The situation in Beiping is calm, but the Japanese concession in Tianjin seems to be preparing for war. However, all the generals have expressed their determination to resist Japan, and the people are also pledging their support. At this time, the entire nation, from top to bottom, should rise up together, refrain from empty talk, and take practical action. Only then will there be a bright future to be seen. I believe that the front lines have considerable strength to resist Japan, but we still need to double our efforts to win the final victory. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

Liang Hancao Discusses the Question of the Ministry of Judicial Administration's Subordination 32

(Nanjing) - Regarding the issue of the Ministry of Judicial Administration's subordination, according to Liang Hancao, the case involves changing the National Government Organization Law, and the Legislative Yuan will carefully review it. Currently, opinions are divided. Some advocate that it should still be under the Executive Yuan, because the functions of judicial administration are to handle administrative matters in the judicial field. Others advocate that it should be changed to be under the Judicial Yuan, because according to the meaning of the five-power separation, the functions of the judiciary should be absolutely independent. If the ministry is considered an administrative agency, then the administrative agencies of other Yuan have not been transferred to the jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan. In terms of advantages and disadvantages, it is irrelevant. I personally have no fixed opinion on this and should wait for the detailed research of the various committees of our Yuan, so as to make it suitable for a reasonable government organization and not violate the spirit of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Supreme Court Encourages the Use of Domestic Goods Association 33

(Nanjing) - The Supreme Court organized the Domestic Goods Association at the end of February, and Ju Zheng appointed Weng Jingtang, Lin Dingzhang, etc. as officials of the association. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Page 9

Constitution Drafting Committee Decides Yesterday 34

Territory, Form of Government, Sovereignty, Flag Colors

Form of Government Set as Republic of the Three Principles of the People

(Nanjing) - The Constitution Drafting Committee held its fourth meeting on the afternoon of the 2nd. Sun Ke chaired the meeting. The following matters were discussed:

(1) Territory: a. Make a general regulation, b. Provinces and regions cannot be changed without the approval of the National Assembly.

(2) Form of Government: The Republic of China is a republic of the Three Principles of the People. (3) Sovereignty: The sovereignty of the Republic of China belongs to all the people of the Republic of China.

(4) Flag colors remain the same (i.e., the current national flag).

It is also reported that the committee will study the issues of people's rights and people's livelihood next week, which will be the responsibility of the Second Group. It is scheduled to meet on the 3rd to review. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) - On the afternoon of the 2nd, the Constitution Drafting Committee discussed the issues of territory, form of government, sovereignty, and flag colors, which were studied during the first week. On the issue of territory, it was decided that (a) of the two principles of enumeration and generalization, generalization should be adopted, and the text should be determined by Wu Jingxiong, Zhang Zhiben, Fu Bingchang, and other drafting committee members. (b) The territory cannot be changed in any way without the resolution of the National Assembly. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

Severe Financial Crisis in the United States 73

Congress to convene special session

The surging tide threatens to engulf the Golden State

Roosevelt consults with new Treasury Secretary on measures

National News Agency, Washington, 1st – The banking crisis and financial situation in the United States has become the most important issue at present. Close associates of the new President Roosevelt have indicated that a special session of Congress will be convened on March 20th. Roosevelt himself met with the new Treasury Secretary Woodin in New York today to discuss urgent measures to stabilize national confidence. In Congress, a bankruptcy bill was passed by a vote of 207 to 26 and sent to the President for signature. The bill allows debtors to apply to the court for a delay in debt repayment to avoid bankruptcy. As for the financial sector, the crisis continues unabated. Even in the Capital District (i.e., the District of Columbia), several banks have restricted withdrawals. Banks in Tennessee and Kentucky have voluntarily closed for five days to discuss effective measures to restrict withdrawals. The legislatures of New Jersey, Delaware, and West Virginia have all passed new laws, with the first two states strictly restricting withdrawals and the latter state authorizing the state government to order banks to close when necessary. Larger banks in Washington are still operating normally and have not experienced difficulties.

National News Agency, New York, 2nd – The financial crisis is spreading and showing no signs of abating. In addition to the voluntary closures of banks in Tennessee and Kentucky, governors in four more states have ordered closures. Banks in California, Oklahoma, and Louisiana have closed for three days each, while Mississippi has closed for ten days. State legislatures are drafting emergency legislation to seek relief. However, this move is largely driven by depositors' panic. The fundamentals of the banks are actually sound. However, at a time when the crisis is raging, government declarations and police warnings cannot stop depositors from withdrawing their funds. Therefore, experienced bankers here believe that the only way to provide emergency relief is to restrict withdrawals until the crisis subsides. It has been reported from Detroit that after a New York bank refused Ford's loan, the First National Bank of that city has rejected Ford's reorganization plan and will continue to operate as before with the current withdrawal restrictions. However, Ford is currently organizing a National Manufacturers Bank to take over the assets of the United Guardian Trust Company.

Reuters, New York, 1st – The developments in the American banking situation over the past 24 hours are still within expectations, as it is known that the unsettled situation will continue to spread. The governor of Alabama has declared a ten-day bank holiday. At the same time, Tennessee and Kentucky have also declared holidays, but these holidays are not mandatory, and many banks in the two states remain open. Four banks in Philadelphia have restricted withdrawals, and a bank in Washington only allows withdrawals of 5% of deposits. Three banks in East St. Louis are also doing the same, with total deposits of 11 million yuan. Small banks in Detroit, Baltimore, and Cleveland have closed, preparing to withdraw large sums of money from the Federal Reserve Bank to meet withdrawals. At the same time, the Reserve Bank also has to deal with a large number of commercial paper discounts, which has led to rumors that the Reserve Bank is being withdrawn. Officials immediately denied this rumor. The interest rate on bank acceptances has risen from 1.25% to 2.25% today. A key figure in New York banking circles stated that New York banks have remitted 500 million yuan in recent weeks to support their correspondent banks and are continuing to do so. New York banks can easily pay depositors' withdrawals, as their average liquidity is about 80%, consisting of cash and readily convertible paper. U.S. government bonds are relatively stable, because banks do not sell the bonds on the market, but hold them to borrow cash from the Reserve Bank. The twenty largest banks in New York currently hold about 450 million yuan in government bonds.

Page 10

Tens of Thousands Expected to Watch Roosevelt's Inauguration Tomorrow 74

National News Agency, Washington, 1st – It is estimated that 200,000 people, including residents of the capital and visitors from all over the country, will attend President Roosevelt's inauguration on Saturday. At least 50,000 of them will be able to witness the new President's inauguration in front of the Capitol, while the rest will gather along Pennsylvania Avenue to watch the new President lead his entourage back to the White House after the inauguration. Representatives from all over the country have already set out, either by car or by special train. The southern states have always supported the Democratic Party, so they have sent many representatives. The western states also supported Roosevelt this time, so their representatives are expected to be numerous as well. The program for the inauguration ceremony has been announced today. It is scheduled that the new President Roosevelt, accompanied by his wife, will arrive at the White House at 11 a.m. on Saturday. He will then travel by car with the outgoing President Hoover, his wife, and several members of Congress to the Capitol. The two Presidents will personally watch Vice President Garner, new Senators, and new Cabinet members take their oaths of office at noon. At 12:50 p.m., President Roosevelt will go to the east side of the Capitol to take his oath of office and deliver his inaugural address. At this time, the army and navy will be lined up on the parade ground, ready for inspection. After the new President holds a luncheon banquet for over 300 guests, he will travel by car to the parade ground near the White House to conduct the inspection. After the formal ceremonies are completed, there will be social celebrations and banquets. The new President and his wife will hold a tea party at the White House to receive 1,500 guests. In the evening, they will host a banquet for 60 distinguished guests at the White House. In addition, the Washington Auditorium will hold a presidential inaugural ball at 10 p.m. As for the outgoing President Hoover, he will quietly leave the Capitol after the new President takes his oath of office and is expected to return to his home in California by car in the evening. There are no special ceremonies regarding the outgoing President.

US New Government Attorney General Dies En Route 75

(Reuters, Wilson, 2nd) Senator Walsh, recently selected by Roosevelt as Attorney General, died suddenly on a train to Washington last night in order to assume office on Saturday. He was found lifeless while sleeping. Walsh had recently married, and he was traveling to the capital to take office with his new wife, who is the daughter of a wealthy Cuban family.

Peru and Japan 76

Reuters, Geneva, 1st – The Council of the League of Nations met tonight for two and a half hours to consider the report of the three-member committee on the Leticia dispute between Peru and Colombia. The committee recommended that Peruvian troops withdraw from the territory and that the League of Nations organize a committee to take over the territory, with Colombian troops maintaining order. However, these troops must be international in nature. The committee believes this is a prerequisite for resolving the dispute. The Colombian representative stated on the spot that he accepted the report and asked Peru to also accept the mediation process, otherwise Peru would be adversely affected under Article 15 of the Covenant. The Council has now authorized the three-member committee to begin drafting a report. Dr. Gu Weijun, the Chinese representative, supported the committee's report and urged both sides to accept it in order to establish a precedent in this turbulent world to maintain peace. The Peruvian representative gave a long speech, comparing the Peruvians to the Japanese, saying that Peru was also moved by the spirit of loyalty to the country and willingness to sacrifice. He also said that Peru upheld the dignity of international obligations and respected treaties, but there was a distinction between honorable and dishonorable treaties, and that all dishonorable treaties should be destroyed. The Peruvian representative then requested a few days of hesitation so that the Peruvian government could consider a reply. Representatives from thirteen countries attended today's Council meeting. The Japanese representative was absent. The chairman did not comment on the matter.

War Debt Negotiations Postponed 77

Reuters, London, 1st – According to news from here today, the war debt negotiations between the UK and the US in Washington must be delayed until April or later. Originally, it was thought that the representatives of both countries could open talks in Washington after Roosevelt took office as President on March 4th. Now, given the many pending matters for the new government, the date of the opening talks has to be postponed. The question of who will be the British representative at the time of the negotiations is also related to the postponement of the opening talks, because the British Finance Minister Chamberlain, who is directly related to the war debt, will be constrained by the budget in April and may not be able to leave the UK.

Japanese Become Like Lunatics When They Encounter War

Mr. Shaw Said He Did Not Regret It

Dentsu, Kobe, 2nd – Shaw, who entered port last night, landed in Kobe at 10 a.m. today to visit the English Quarter and Motomachi in the city. Japan also needs to limit the number of births. He landed at 4:30 p.m. to watch a play at the Kabuki-za in Osaka.

British and American Military Spending 79

Reuters, Washington, 2nd – The US Senate passed the naval budget for 1934 today, but the Senate reduced the amount passed by the House of Representatives, 315,419,000 gold yuan, to 308,000,000 gold yuan. The bill has now been sent back to the House.

Reuters, London, 2nd – The British army budget totals 37,950,000 pounds, an increase of 1,462,000 pounds over last year. The number of soldiers will remain at 148,700. The British standing army, including the British army stationed in India, is currently 5,000 people short of the quota, compared to 8,000 people short last year. However, the British army in India must be increased to the full quota.

Progress of the Disarmament Conference 80

National News Agency, Geneva, 1st – The General Commission of the Disarmament Conference made an important resolution at its meeting today: all professional armies whose service years are longer than the militia, except for the troops needed for joint military actions by the League of Nations, must be prohibited. Germany is paying close attention to this, because according to this resolution, if Germany adopts the militia system, then the national defense force will no longer exist.

Reuters, Geneva, 1st – The Aviation Committee of the Disarmament Conference today passed a motion clearly stipulating that the committee's work is based entirely on the assumption of the complete abolition of the army, navy, air force, and anti-aircraft. It is expected that after this resolution, Germany will be able to participate in the discussions of the Aviation Committee in the future. The general opinion on the issue of the internationalization of the Air Police Force is conditioned on the acceptance of the complete abolition of the army, navy, and air force. Indian representative Wheeler claimed that he anticipated serious difficulties in internationalizing the aviation industry within India and between India and England. (Geneva) The Japanese representative to Switzerland, Yada, met with the chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, this afternoon and informed him that the Japanese government had decided to continue to participate in the work of the Disarmament Conference. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

"Aerial Motorcycle" 81

(Reuters, London Correspondence) – A new type of aircraft will soon appear on the market. The aircraft is propelled by a six-horsepower engine and is very easy to drive and very safe, so it can also be called an "aerial motorcycle." Ten years ago, Linpu had tried it, but the basic structure of the machine focused on achieving rapid and durable flight with very little horsepower. The new aircraft has a maximum speed of 50 miles per hour and a gliding speed of 18 miles per hour, just like a "small car" among aircraft. This type of aircraft is ideal for recreation in good weather, and the value of each aircraft is about 250 pounds.

Rehe in Wartime 82

Reuters Reporter Inspects Rehe

Foreigners Claim Chinese Troops Defend Natural Defenses

Gubeikou Communication, 27th – Although the situation outside the pass is unknown, the ice and snow inside the pass have begun to melt. A Reuters reporter rode to Chengde and did not see any signs of war along the way. It was not until Miyun that he saw troops. The [illegible] Division is stationed in the area between Miyun and Gubeikou. Livestock used for military transportation, such as mules, horses, and camels, are everywhere and seem to be sufficient. The food stored along the way is also very abundant. The reporter asked the villagers about the war and what they thought. They all stared blankly and did not know how to respond, saying that they had not heard of any war. The morale of the troops is excellent, and they are well-fed, well-clothed, and have sufficient ammunition. Their discipline is also good. They pay generously for food and other items purchased from villagers along the way and are courteous to travelers. On the way to Gubeikou, he saw a large group of camels transporting ammunition to Rehe. The reporter met several foreign travelers returning from Rehe in Gubeikou. One of them claimed that the areas defended by Zhang Xueliang's troops are all natural defenses. If the supply of ammunition is uninterrupted and there is a determination to resist the enemy, they may not be able to hold out for long, but they can last for a long time. (Reuters)

Japanese Merchants in Yuguan Refuse to Declare and Pay Taxes 83

Report from the Customs Officer of Qinhuangdao

Sir Frederick Maze, Inspector General of Customs, stated that several days ago, according to a telegram from the customs officer of Qinhuangdao, Japanese merchants in Yuguan have refused to comply with the regulations and declare and pay taxes at Chinese customs since February 4th. After several weeks, a serious protest was lodged with the Japanese Consul in Tianjin. It has been found that the Yuguan Customs branch is located within the Great Wall and is still under the jurisdiction of the Chinese government. The customs duties collected by the branch, like the taxes collected at other treaty ports, are used in accordance with the treaty as security for the debt repayments to various countries. Japan is also one of the creditors of the debt repayments. The merchants of that country have violated the treaty, and if this behavior is not strictly corrected, the integrity and status of the customs, in which all countries have an interest, will inevitably be affected. (National News Agency)

Liu Chongjie Returns from Inspecting Shihe 84

Substituting for Song Ziwen in慰勞ing the Frontline Soldiers

Although the Soldiers Endured Hardship, They Were Extremely Brave

Beiping Correspondence: Liu Chongjie, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, and Shang Zhen departed from Beiping on the Beining Special Train at 1:00 AM on the 25th to慰勞 the frontline soldiers at Shihe. After completing their mission on the evening of the 26th, they took a train from Qinhuangdao back west and arrived in Beiping at 10:10 AM on the 27th. That afternoon at 4:00 PM, they met with reporters at the Foreign Affairs Building to discuss the situation. The details are recorded as follows: "President Song previously came to Beiping and went to Rehe to慰勞 the soldiers. For the Shihe front, he dispatched me to represent him in慰勞ing and inspecting. I, along with Chief Commander Shang, left Beiping at 1:00 AM on Friday night and first arrived at certain locations to慰勞 the troops under Chief Commander Shang. Then, I went to various frontline locations in the defense area of Army Commander He Zhuguo to慰勞 and inspect the defense work. The weather on the front line is still cold, but the morale is high. Although they endure hardship, everyone is united, and their bravery has not diminished. They are ready to fight the enemy when they can no longer bear it. Every soldier has this determination. Although we are not as well-equipped as the enemy in terms of weapons and supplies, our spirit is far superior to theirs. I met with Regiment Commander Shi Shian and inquired about the situation during the Yuguan Incident. The enemy's provocation was obvious. If the enemy had not climbed the city walls, we would not have been able to defend ourselves. This is a past matter, and there is no need to elaborate further. In addition, I also explained the situation of the League of Nations to the frontline soldiers, saying that only with a spirit of sacrifice can one obtain justice. They understand this quite well. Army Commander He Zhuguo expressed an even stronger determination to resist the enemy. In short, during this inspection, I deeply respected the frontline soldiers. The people in the rear should also have the spirit of enduring hardship and hunger of the frontline soldiers and dedicate themselves to assisting the front. If the front falls, the rear must continue the fight. There has been no fighting on the front line recently. Yesterday (the 26th), five Japanese warships were docked in Qinhuangdao, including two cruisers and three destroyers. In the Yuguan area, the enemy is constantly preparing. If we do not fight desperately in the future, there will be no way out. Currently, Rehe is in an emergency. Everyone should not only focus on Rehe but also remember the Shihe front. The invisible urgency there is similar to that in Rehe. I will leave Beiping in the next few days to return south. I plan to first go to Nanjing to report to President Song and Minister Luo and then decide on my future actions. If necessary, I may come north again." When reporters asked about the truth of the Japanese propaganda regarding the discovery of Chinese military aircraft in Shanhaiguan and how diplomatic relations would be handled if the enemy threatened Beiping and Tianjin, he replied, "The Japanese claim about the discovery of aircraft in Shanhaiguan is, of course, another propaganda tactic, which is easy to understand. At present, we can only wait for their aircraft and artillery to come and fight them. The Yuguan Incident has already violated the Boxer Protocol. If they threaten Beiping and Tianjin in the future, we can only defend our territory and, at the same time, notify the signatory countries of the Boxer Protocol and ask them to fulfill their treaty obligations." (28th)

Establishment of the New Hubei Provincial Government 85

The Newly Appointed Directors of the Four Departments Take Office Simultaneously

Hankou Correspondence: The new Hubei Provincial Government was officially established on March 1st. The members and chairman are Xia Douyin, concurrently serving as the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs; Li Shucheng, concurrently serving as the Director of the Department of Finance; Jia Shiyi, concurrently serving as the Director of the Department of Construction; Li Fanyi, concurrently serving as the Director of the Department of Education; Cheng Tianfang. The members are Yang Zaichun, Chen Daxun, and Wu Guozhen. The Secretary-General is Jiang Youwen. They were sworn into office at the same time. Zhu Shaoliang was sent by the Central Government, and Zhong Yancheng was sent by the Executive Yuan of the National Government to supervise the oath-taking. Many guests attended the ceremony, including Cao Haosen, Chief of Staff of the Headquarters, and Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General. The meeting opened at 10:00 AM. After Chairman Xia Douyin performed the ceremony, Zhu Shaoliang presented the seals of office. Xia and the four department directors, Li, Jia, Li, and Cheng, each received their seals of office separately. After all the members took the oath, Zhu Shaoliang delivered a speech, stating that Hubei Province had suffered from natural disasters and man-made calamities for many years, and the people were suffering greatly, like a patient with a disease that had penetrated deep into the marrow. The members were like doctors who had come to treat the disease, but a good doctor must first investigate the source of the disease before prescribing the right medicine. The source of Hubei's disease was not only caused by bandits, but also by widespread corruption and the failure to focus on fundamental education. In the future, in order to restore order, it is necessary to provide relief to the unemployed, improve education, ensure that reality matches reputation, and cultivate integrity. As the saying goes, "Governance does not lie in many words but in vigorous action." He hoped that all members would work hard. Then, Shi Yancheng delivered a speech, stating that when the Commander-in-Chief was in Hubei, he stipulated that three parts of military force and seven parts of political force should be used to eliminate the Red bandits. Now, the military suppression of bandits has come to an end, and he hoped that all members would work hard to complete the political construction. Next, Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Headquarters, Yu Yuzhi, member of the Provincial Party Department, Fang Benren, a gentry, and He Hengfu, a representative of the Hankou Chamber of Commerce, delivered speeches successively. Finally, Xia Douyin delivered a reply, stating that Hubei is located in the center of the country, controls the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and has suffered frequent disasters, leading to a decline in vitality. Recently, due to the outbreak of the war in Rehe, foreign troubles are becoming more urgent. The provincial government has a heavy responsibility and is not something that his colleagues can handle alone. However, driven by a sense of responsibility, he cannot but bravely accept the arduous task. In addition to following the instructions of the Central Government and respecting the leadership of the Commander-in-Chief in eliminating corruption and diligently seeking the welfare of the people, he also hopes that the elders of the local community will cooperate to adapt to this severe situation. After Xia finished speaking, music was played, and the meeting adjourned.

On the 1st, the four departments of civil affairs, finance, construction, and education simultaneously dispatched personnel to take over. Li Shucheng, Jia Shiyi, Li Fanyi, and Cheng Tianfang all went to their respective departments to take office. They gathered all the staff for a speech and announced the appointment of important officials. Wang Shiyu and Zhu Yizhou were appointed as secretaries of the Department of Civil Affairs; Xiong Daorui, Jiang Jie, and Peng Guangxuan were appointed as assistant secretaries; Fan Hongtai, Hu Zhongmin, Wang Kaihua, and Cheng Hongshu were appointed as section chiefs. Wu Longxun was appointed as the secretary-general of the Department of Finance; Wang Ruyi was appointed as the secretary; Ren Chaowen, Xue Guangxun, He Xizhang, and Gui Jingqiu were appointed as section chiefs. It is said that more than 80 people were laid off. Qiu Zhize was appointed as the secretary and acting chief of the first section of the Department of Construction; Chen Cong was appointed as the technician and acting chief of the second section; Lu Bo was appointed as the secretary and acting chief of the third section; Zhang Yanxiang was appointed as the technician and acting chief of the fourth section. Chen Yingkun and Fang Shanzheng were appointed as secretaries of the Department of Education; Deng Bixing, Chen Jitang, and Wang Dexi were appointed as section chiefs. Li Shucheng stated that the most important tasks of the Department of Civil Affairs are to improve county governments, strengthen personnel, and conduct land surveys. There are many other matters to be handled, and he will strive to implement them in accordance with the laws and regulations of the headquarters. Jia Shiyi stated that Hubei's finances have no source to open up, and reductions have already been implemented. In the future, the main goal will be to maintain the status quo and gradually reorganize. The business tax issue is consistent nationwide, and Hubei cannot be unique. He plans to thoroughly rectify it. Cheng Tianfang stated that Hubei's education funding is extremely difficult. Since the reduction, it has been barely able to support itself. During this time of national crisis, we should still strive to be thrifty.

After the establishment of the new provincial government, a telegram was sent to the Central Government, the National Government, and the Executive Yuan for record, and a telegram was sent to all parties, stating, "According to the order of the National Government, Xia Douyin, Li Shucheng, Jia Shiyi, Li Fanyi, Cheng Tianfang, Fan Xiji, Yang Zaichun, Chen Daxun, and Wu Guozhen are appointed as members of the Hubei Provincial Government, and Xia Douyin is appointed as the chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, Li Shucheng is appointed as the director of the Department of Civil Affairs of the Hubei Provincial Government, Jia Shiyi is appointed as the director of the Department of Finance of the Hubei Provincial Government, Li Fanyi is appointed as the director of the Department of Construction of the Hubei Provincial Government, and Cheng Tianfang is appointed as the director of the Department of Education of the Hubei Provincial Government. Following this order, we were sworn into office on March 1st. Hubei is located in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and the safety of the entire country depends on it. Frequent disasters have left wounds unhealed, and the national crisis is deepening, and the Red atmosphere needs to be quelled. Douyin and others have wrongly accepted the heavy responsibility and are deeply ashamed of their meager talents. We are alarmed by the great difficulties ahead and are constantly cautious. We hope that the grand plans will be far-reaching and that instructions will be frequently issued so that we can follow them and avoid failure. We hereby send a telegram for your information. Respectfully awaiting your instructions. Xia Douyin, Li Shucheng, Jia Shiyi, Cheng Tianfang, Fan Xiji, Yang Zaichun, Chen Daxun, Wu Guozhen bow to the east." However, member Fan Xiji was still supervising the suppression of bandits in western Hubei, so he did not participate in the inauguration of the other members and will be sworn in after his triumphant return. (March 1st)

Songjiang

Chamber of Commerce Executives Retain Chairman

Cai Guangyao, the chairman of the county chamber of commerce, concurrently holds many positions in local public organizations, and his duties are numerous and busy. Recently, feeling that he is unable to cope with the demands of his age, he invited the standing committee members of the chamber of commerce and local officials and leaders the other day, stating that he would resign from all his positions. Although they unanimously persuaded him to stay at the time, his attitude was extremely firm. He transferred the chamber of commerce funds and documents to the standing committee members for receipt. Today (the 2nd) at 1:00 PM, the county chamber of commerce convened a joint meeting of executives and supervisors, and unanimously voted to retain the chairman. Zhang Mengxing, Zhang Qingquan, Zhu Yian, and four others were elected as representatives to visit and persuade him to stay. It was also resolved to telegraph the central government not to renew the Sino-Japanese Reciprocal Tariff Treaty and to vigorously resist Japanese goods in order to demonstrate public sentiment.

Property Management Office Requests Reduction of Additional Grain Taxes Again

The County Property Management Office previously telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, requesting that the penalty for late payment of winter grain taxes this year be reduced by two yuan in additional grain taxes to alleviate the people's difficulties, which was indeed a matter of compassion. Later, it received a reply from the Ministry, instructing the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to make earnest corrections. Recently, because the Finance Bureau still calculates the arrearage at 7 yuan and 9 jiao of silver per shi (unit of dry measure), including a 2-yuan arrearage penalty, the office telegraphed the Ministry again yesterday, requesting that the Department of Finance be instructed to order the Finance Bureau to correct it immediately to benefit the people and demonstrate great integrity.

Kunshan

Exhibition of Anti-Japanese War Relics Opens

Last year, during the anti-Japanese war in Shanghai, this county was bombed by Japanese aircraft. A year has passed, and the Japanese invaders have invaded Rehe again. In order to arouse the public to unite against Japan, the Public Education Center held an exhibition of relics from the anti-Japanese war in Shanghai starting on the 1st. In addition to borrowing military supplies seized from the Japanese army during the war from the Public Education Center in Shanghai and the March 1st Museum in Taicang, the county party headquarters and chamber of commerce also sent various types of Japanese artillery shells and superstitious objects to be displayed in the hall of the center. From morning to night, visitors streamed in an endless flow. The exhibition will last for five days.

Bandits Rob Dashu Town

Dashu Town in the county is located in a remote area and is often disturbed by lake bandits. Last month, a large gang of lake bandits arrived there and stayed for a while, but fortunately, they did not rob anyone. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, another bandit ship arrived there, with more than a dozen bandits on board, each armed with guns. After landing, they first cut the telephone lines, then searched door to door. After an hour, no shop or household in the whole town was spared. The bandits boarded their ship after robbing and left with a roar. Afterwards, the town chief, Ren Yi, reported to the Zhangpu Public Security Branch, which reported to the county government for strict investigation.

Suzhou

Criminals Involved in Opium Seizure Case

Transferred to Jiangsu High Court for Trial

Zhang Shaoyi, the director of the stolen goods section of the third section of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, seized a large amount of opium. After being discovered by Mayor Wu, he was sent to the Shanghai Court, which sentenced Zhang to four years and six months in prison and fined him 2,000 yuan. Police officer Wu Deyu and bailiff Ji Asi were declared innocent. Zhang refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. The prosecutor in the original trial also refused to accept the acquittal of Wu and Ji and filed an appeal. Yesterday (the 2nd), the Shanghai Court transferred Zhang, Wu, Ji, and the entire case file to the Jiangsu High Court and sent them to prison for custody, with a hearing scheduled.

A Series of Instructions from the High Court

The High Court issued the following instructions yesterday: (1) All county courts should uniformly produce tables of suspects and prisoners. (2) Prison vans should be used to transport prisoners to the capital. (3) Each county may not transport more than 12 prisoners at a time. (4) Male and female prisoners and minors from each county should be transported separately. (5) The bail of the defendant should be sent to the receiving prison together at the time of execution.

Wuxi

Record of Party-Government Talks

The county party headquarters held its fifth party-government talks yesterday, chaired by Li Tiping. Matters discussed: (1) A letter from the Special Party Department of the 88th Division of the Army stated that Japanese people have established large-scale grain storage facilities in major ports in Tianjin, Shanghai, and Hankou to purchase Chinese grain and that strict prevention should be enforced to prevent theft and leakage. How should this case be handled? Resolution: (A) It is recommended to the province that it quickly formulate preventive measures to prevent smuggling. (B) Local water and land military police should strictly prevent smuggling at all times. (2) The provincial party headquarters forwarded four types of methods for setting up radios in various places and ordered them to be followed. How should this case be handled? Resolution: It is returned to the county government for consideration and handling. (3) The Wuxi All-Circles Aviation Patriotic Work Promotion Method was approved, and the county party headquarters, county government, and county chamber of commerce were contacted to establish a board of directors as soon as possible to carry out fundraising in earnest. (Omissions)

Yarn Industry Funds Used to Purchase Aircraft

Since the "September 18th Incident" two years ago, the dyeing and weaving industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang has been actively resisting foreign yarn and striving to develop self-spun fine yarn. For each piece of yarn used, a yarn industry fund must be collected. The accumulated amount has now reached more than 90,000 yuan. Yesterday, the Wuxi Cloth Factory Guild telegraphed the standing committee members of the Shanghai Jiangsu-Zhejiang Dyeing and Weaving Industry Federation, Zhu Wenqi and Cui Fuzhuang, requesting that relevant industries in the two provinces be convened immediately to use this money to purchase an aircraft, which would be named the "Jiangsu-Zhejiang Dyeing and Weaving Aircraft" to promote the industry. At the same time, telegraphs were sent to the same industries in Wujin, Changshu, Wuxian, and other places, unanimously advocating the plan. In addition, the county party headquarters, together with the county government and the county chamber of commerce, discussed and resolved the aviation patriotic promotion method, and a board of directors was established as soon as possible to carry out fundraising for aviation patriotic funds in earnest.

Changzhou

County Government Dispatches Personnel to Take Over the Construction Bureau

The Wuyi Construction Bureau was ordered to be abolished, and all its undertakings were taken over by the county government, which established a section to continue handling them. After receiving the order, the bureau closed everything and handed it over yesterday (the 1st). County Chief Zhang specially dispatched Qian Tangxin and Wang Maoxin to take over. At the same time, the personnel of the county government's technical office were announced, including Xu Jiamo, the director of the technical office, Xiang Jie, Zhu Fuyuan, and Ni Liang, technicians, and Li Wenxue and Su Liusheng, clerks, who were all reappointed from the original staff of the Construction Bureau and will report to the government office within days.

Changshu

Farmer Dies of Illness in Prison

Last year, the agricultural harvest was abundant, but because of low grain prices, farmers were greatly affected. In addition, due to years of famine, landlords pressed for rent even more. Farmers were overwhelmed by debt and found it difficult to cope. As a result, there were countless cases of landlords imprisoning tenants who failed to pay rent. According to a survey last winter, there were more than 500 tenants in custody. The detention center was overcrowded, which was detrimental to hygiene. There have been several cases of illness. The other day, Zhang Sengui, a farmer from Mochen Township, owed rent to a certain family and was imprisoned on December 31st last year. Zhang was already 56 years old and became ill after being imprisoned. There was also a lack of medical care in the prison, so he died of illness in prison on the 28th of last month. After the prison clerk reported to the county government for verification, the family of the deceased was notified to come to the county to collect the body.

Jiangyin

Five Female Prisoners Escape from Detention Center

The county prison's detention center held eight female prisoners whose cases had not been decided. The guard, Aunt Liu, was over fifty years old. Yesterday (the 1st) at around 5:00 PM, she followed the usual procedure and locked up the prisoners. Unexpectedly, Yan Wangshi, a bandit from Jingjiang, and Li Wangshi (six months' imprisonment), Xu Soshi (ten years' imprisonment), Qiu Zhangshi (five years' imprisonment), and He Chenshi (a major criminal accused of murdering her husband, He Yunlin), five prisoners whose cases had not been decided, tied up their fellow prisoners Sun Caodi, Dai Caishi, Yang Yushi, and the female guard, Aunt Liu, with strips of cloth torn from their clothes, forced them to hand over the keys, and opened the door to escape. At around 10:00 PM that night, prison officer Chen learned of the incident and urgently reported it to the county government's public security bureau police team, which searched everywhere, but there was no trace of the five female prisoners. That night, Acting County Chief Wang urgently telegraphed Zheng and other counties to assist in the arrest.

Zhenjiang

Recent Survey of Japanese Warships and Merchant Ships

According to a recent survey, there are a total of fourteen Japanese residents in Zhenjiang. There is currently one Japanese warship, the "Suko Kai," a cruiser, on the river. There were formerly ten Japanese commercial vessels on the Yangtze River. After the war in Shanghai, the Luoyang, Fengyang, Nanyang, and Xiangyang vessels were equipped to transport 200-300 tons of cargo each time, incurring a loss of about 2,000 yuan each time. The reason why they continue to sail as usual is only to maintain the route.

Taicang

Construction of Dike Banks to Begin on Schedule

The dike banks along the river in the first, sixth, and eighth districts of this county have been collapsing more and more due to years of disrepair. Every time there is a tide, the fields and crops are submerged, resulting in poor harvests at the end of autumn and huge losses. In order to prevent this from happening, the county government is levying labor to repair them. Construction is scheduled to begin on March 6th and will last for one month. The dike bank system will have an outer dike width of 1.67 meters and an inner dike width of 1.33 meters, with a height of 30 centimeters above the water surface.

Gaoyou

Yunhe Engineering Bureau Surveys Waterway to the Sea

The Jiangbei Yunhe Engineering Bureau has now dispatched survey team leader Zhang Bin, Li to lead more than twenty surveyors to survey the waterway to the sea. The surveyors arrived in You yesterday and are stationed at the Huayan Temple outside the South Gate. They will start surveying eastward from the Chenan Xinguilai Sanba starting point.

Hangzhou

Hangyu Company Officially Operated by the Government

The Hangyu Road Automobile Company was ordered to be reorganized due to poor management. As the Department of Construction's efforts to improve it were ineffective, it was decided to take it back and operate it officially. The company had previously suffered operating losses of more than 90,000 yuan. The Department of Construction first paid 100,000 yuan in cash yesterday based on the assessed price, and 75,000 yuan in government bonds. The remaining 25,000 yuan in cash will also be allocated by the department soon.

Xiaoshan

Wind and Rain Cause Disaster, Boats Sink

There was wind and rain on February 28th, which was even worse at night. Countless boats along the river sank due to the strong wind and waves. Two paper cargo boats and one jar boat that had come from Shangjiang that night suddenly sank because their masts were blown off by the wind. Nine boatmen drowned, and two died. The paper cargo and jars were all sunk in the middle of the river, with losses exceeding 5,000 yuan. Also, the tide was stirred up by the wind, and many houses along the river collapsed.

Mingguang

Security Team Defeats Bandit Gang

The county security team reported yesterday from the Shiba district that there were hundreds of bandits in the Dayaoying area who were attempting to flee south. After receiving the report, squadron leader Yang Jianping led his team at night to block and intercept them. At dawn on the 27th, they made contact with the bandits in the Duangou area and engaged in a fierce battle all day. At dusk, the bandits escaped through a small path. Squadron Leader Yang is now planning to join forces with the Gangtai Security Team to investigate and take action together.

Local News

Acting Chairman Lang Guen-p'u and Others Arrive in Shanghai 86

About to go to Beijing to report on the anti-Japanese campaign.

Rumor has it that Su Ma has already returned home via Western Europe.

The Northeast Volunteer Army's strength remains extremely formidable.

Lang Guen-p'u, the Acting Chairman and Director of Finance of Heilongjiang Province, Zhou Weitai, the Director of Industry, Zhou Deyu, the Secretary-General, He Yin, the Confidential Secretary, You Sui, the Chief Secretary, Zhang Linsui, the Chief of Staff of the Deputy Commander-in-Chief's Office, Wu Yuandan, the Adjutant, Li Pizu, the Chief of the General Staff Office, Wang Binqing, the member of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and over forty others, arrived in Shanghai on the Soviet Russian cargo ship "Tongli" on the 27th. Mr. Lang is scheduled to go to Beijing next week to report to the central government on the situation in the Northeast. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited Mr. Zhou Weitai at his residence yesterday and learned about the hardships encountered by Mr. Zhou and his party on their way to Shanghai. The details are as follows:

Difficult Journey: According to them, after retreating from Heihe, they inquired about the way to Vladivostok. Fortunately, they were able to borrow vacant rooms at our consulate in Vladivostok to survive hunger and cold. There used to be Japanese ships traveling between Vladivostok and Shanghai every week, but it was certain that they would encounter trouble. Therefore, they decided to take a Russian ship to Shanghai. However, Russian ships carried cargo but not passengers. After much negotiation, they were finally allowed to board. However, the "Tongli" ship, which was originally scheduled to come to Shanghai on January 18, did not depart for Shanghai until around February 20, a delay of more than thirty days. The forty people traveling together endured countless hardships on this cargo ship.

Anti-Japanese Troops: Among the anti-Japanese troops who retreated into Russian territory, there were over two thousand troops under Su Bingwen and over one thousand troops under Li Du and Wang Delin. As for Chairman Ma's troops, they have been handed over to his subordinates, and the current situation is unclear. As for the Volunteer Army lurking in the mountains and forests of the Eastern Provinces, there are still forty to fifty thousand men. Although they are able to avoid hunger and cold, they lack bullets and their strength is not great. Fortunately, the people of the Northeast have always maintained close ties with the Volunteer Army. If there is a shortage of supplies needed by the Volunteer Army, they will do their best to provide them. If our army launches an expedition out of the Pass in the future, it may not be a helping hand.

Ding Chao Loses Integrity: As for Ding Chao, he did not retreat into Russian territory, nor was he arrested. It is said that he has surrendered to the puppet state, which is regrettable for his late-life integrity. As for those who did not share the same goals among the forty people who came south, we can only let them be.

Su Ma's Whereabouts

When we were in Vladivostok, we heard that Generals Su Bingwen and Ma Zhanshan had already passed through Moscow and were returning home via Western Europe by ship from France. However, when we arrived in Shanghai, there was no news of them. Currently, Wu Huanzhang, Mr. Ma's representative in Shanghai, has already telegraphed Deputy Chairman Zhang in Peiping and the National Government in Nanking to inquire about the whereabouts of the two gentlemen. As of today, no reply has been received. Mr. Lang will go to Beijing: We felt quite tired after arriving in Shanghai, so we are taking a short rest here. Acting Chairman Lang will go to Beijing next week to report to the central government on the situation in the three northeastern provinces. It is undecided whether we will go to Beijing or not.

Reflecting on the Past: He finally said that during the Battle of Nenjiang Bridge led by General Ma and the Battle of Hailar led by General Su, the Japanese forces in the Eastern Provinces had not yet been firmly established, and the strength of the Volunteer Army was also extremely formidable. If our army could resist the enemy and leave the Pass, we could attack from both sides, and the Japanese would be exhausted. Although we could not completely annihilate the enemy, we could certainly inflict heavy losses. Unified command and fighting against the enemy to recover the three northeastern provinces was not without a glimmer of hope. Now it's all over.

Zhou Weitai's Talk: This time, I came to Shanghai from Heihe and plan to go to Peiping to visit my relatives. I will not stay long. I regret that I failed to carry out my original intention in supporting Chairman Ma's anti-Japanese campaign. I have failed the government's trust and the people's expectations. Since things have changed, I do not want to express any opinions to others. Now that I have been honored with an interview and appreciated your good intentions, I will summarize my personal experience and answer. As for the military actions and various plans over the past year, and the reasons for the ultimate failure to save the situation, the details are complicated and cannot be fully explained in a few words, nor can they be answered by me alone. I will not go into details here.

Heihe Gold Mine: In the eighth year of the Republic of China, I founded the Heihe Fengyuan Gold Mine, which has been fifteen years ago. When I was serving as an official in various provinces before, I was young and strong and eager to make achievements. However, the situation was turbulent and there was no peace. Therefore, I made it my mission not to enter the political arena and to develop industry in the border areas. Therefore, I would not enter the provincial capital unless there was an important official matter to discuss. When Military Governor Wu Xingquan was in charge of Jiang Province, he repeatedly tried to keep me in important positions, but I politely declined, because I did not want to change my original intention. In April of last year, Chairman Ma and his colleagues came to Heihe. Since he had known me well when he was the commander of the garrison, he offered me the position of provincial commissioner. Because I could not refuse firmly, I took the position of industry on the condition that I would not receive a salary and that I would be allowed to resign after the lost territories were recovered. When Chairman Ma led his troops on an expedition, he also ordered me to concurrently serve as the head of civil affairs and police.

Acting Chairman Lang: At that time, Lang Juchen, as the Director of Finance, acted as the Chairman, and Xu Qingshan, as the Commander of the Garrison, acted as the Deputy Commander. Xu was an old subordinate of Chairman Ma, while Lang and Chairman Ma were close friends, and I was a long-time friend of both of them. Military and civilian affairs were concentrated in Heihe, making it a fundamental and important place. The responsibility for maintaining the situation was jointly borne by the three of us. We discussed everything with each other, and when there were differences of opinion between the military and civilians, we always used compromise methods to mediate and maintain the overall situation. Therefore, we were able to get along harmoniously from beginning to end.

Supporting Nine Months: Finance is the lifeline of the military. All personnel and administrative matters must be based on fundraising. Heihe has no income, except for the gold produced by the Fengyuan and Xing'an factories, which are operated by merchants, to stimulate the market. At that time, the needs were huge and there was no way to raise funds. Therefore, in the name of the original official silver house, banknotes were issued, and they were circulated far and wide by relying on the proceeds from the two sales of gold. At that time, if banknotes were not issued, it would be like cooking without rice, and without the cash from the two factories, it would be like water without a source. We were able to support it for nine months because of this.

Heihe Transportation: In winter and spring, Heihe is connected to Bu Kui by land, and in summer and autumn, it is connected to Harbin by water. Merchants travel back and forth in an endless stream, and food and goods are imported by boat and car. Since the military uprising, both land and water routes have been blocked by the enemy. The limited food reserves caused great panic. Therefore, a food maintenance association was established to distribute food according to the population. Various methods were used to purchase and transport food from various counties in the south. If that was not enough, food was purchased from Russian territory. Since I have been living in the border area for a long time, I have considerable feelings for all parties and can still be trusted. Therefore, what the government could not do was done in the name of merchants or individuals. The same was done for various materials. The difficulties encountered cannot be overstated. It was almost a miracle that we did not fall into a desperate situation.

Self-Made Wooden Wheels: The Heilongjiang River freezes in winter, and can only be used for transportation in summer and autumn. However, there are few sailboats, and they are extremely slow. It takes more than a month to travel back and forth from Heihe to the area north of Qikluo. In the summer of last year, we considered this and, in the midst of a lack of everything, we recruited merchant shareholders and collected materials to build a wooden ship called Hailanpao to transport grain and goods, so that we would not have to worry. The travelers also praised its convenience. Hailanpao is the original name of Heihe, so it was named after it.

Sparse Population: Heihe is more than 50 li along the border, with a sparse population. Robbers and thieves appear and disappear unpredictably, causing trouble for a long time. Moreover, during this eventful time, the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted. Those who become bandits are especially numerous. The responsibility for maintaining security is the exclusive responsibility of the police. Therefore, the Heihe Public Security Bureau was reorganized to ensure the safety of the market. In winter, a security team of 240 people was established. The necessary guns, ammunition, and rations were jointly raised by the government and merchants. Several groups of bandits were wiped out before they could spread. Recently, people from Heihe who came to Shanghai continued to talk about the security situation there, saying that if it were not for this move, it would have become a bandit area.

Unity and Consistency: All of the above-mentioned tasks of maintaining the rear area were my duty. Even though I repeatedly used my family's assets to subsidize military expenses, and this time I left Heihe and sacrificed the mineral resources that I had managed for many years and the various businesses that I had prepared, the losses were indeed great, but since it was a matter of saving the country, it was not worth mentioning. However, due to the lack of weapons and soldiers, and the lack of support from the surrounding areas, we were unable to sustain it in the end. We had no choice but to return to the country by way of a detour. Although the people of the country can understand our difficulties, we deeply regret it when we look back. Now, the situation in the north is becoming more and more dangerous. The previous vehicle has overturned, and the coming cart is coming. How should we unite as one and work together to crush the strong power and recover the lost territories, so as to avoid falling into a state of immunity to death? Looking forward to the future, what I hope all the people of the country will work together to achieve.

City Federation Issues Letters

To Promote Wartime Organizations

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation yesterday sent letters to organizations such as the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Local Association, the Shanghai General Labor Union, and the Shanghai All Roads Business Federation, saying: "Dear Sirs, the national situation is getting more and more dangerous. The news from Rehe is even worse than before. The military officers in the north are still living in extravagance and luxury, and neglecting border defense. If we do not seek remedies urgently, it will be more than enough to lead to national subjugation and racial extinction. It is not too late to attempt it now. The country is the accumulation of the people. There is no government that is scattered without the scattering of the people. Shanghai is the center of culture and the important town of economy. If we say that there are no organizations, then the names can be changed and counted. If we say that they are not scattered, then the work of saving the country is divided. Our association has learned from this and issued a declaration to advise all the citizens of the city on February 24, especially to promote the wartime organization as the first righteousness, believing that if the citizens of Shanghai can move together, then all the people can move together, and if all the people can move together, then the government can move together. Our association's purpose is to save the country, and we do not want to take the lead in success, and we do not dare to fall behind in responsibility. We have always adhered to this purpose. We only see that the declaration has been issued for a few days, and letting virtue can be the wind. Therefore, we do not measure our strength and act as pioneers. If we are approved, we would like to follow. Time waits for no one, please show us the way forward. Corresponding letters are requested to be checked and replied to."

Zang Qifang's Speech: Hot War and Recovering the Northeast 87

We must fight desperately to defend the land that has not been lost.

Continue to mobilize the people to fight hard.

丨Speech at the Youth Association the day before yesterday丨

The Central News Agency reported that since the outbreak of the war in Rehe, people across the country have been paying attention. The Shanghai Baxianqiao Youth Association specially launched a lecture series on the Rehe issue, inviting Mr. Xiong Xiling, Huang Yanpei, and Zang Qifang, who had just arrived in Shanghai from North China, to speak for three days starting on the 1st. The day before yesterday was the first day, with speeches by Mr. Huang Yanpei and Zang Qifang. There was a large audience. The following is a record of Zang's speech:

After September 18th: I just listened to Mr. Huang Renzhi's speech on the situation in Rehe, and how the people of the whole country should work hard to achieve the goal of preserving Rehe and recovering the Northeast. This is something that everyone should not forget every moment. Now I will talk to you about the situation in the Northeast from the September 18th Incident to the present. The reason why we have to defend Rehe to the death now is to recover the Northeast in the future. The Rehe issue was caused by the Northeast issue, so our eyes should be on the Northeast when the Rehe military situation is urgent.

How Should We: Now Japan is concentrating its forces to attack Rehe because they believe that the Northeast Volunteer Army has been wiped out and there is no worry about the rear. Attacking Rehe is to preserve the Northeast. This is Japan's plan. What should we do? We should mobilize the people of the Northeast who have always resisted Japan, so that they believe that the "wiped out" have not really been wiped out. On the one hand, we should disrupt their rear, so that their original plan cannot be realized. On the other hand, we should contain their forces, so that our Rehe can be guarded more firmly. Therefore, at present, in addition to concentrating the strength of the whole country to support Rehe, we should not forget the Northeast, that is, we should carry out resistance and recovery work at the same time. Below, I will divide the situation in the Northeast after the September 18th Incident into five periods to explain.

First Period: The first period is from the September 18th Incident to the Jiangqiao Battle, that is, from September 18th to November 4th of the tenth year. The Shenyang Incident occurred on the night of September 18th. Changchun, Kaiyuan, Tieling, Sipingjie and other places along the South Manchuria Railway were occupied at the same time. Until the 21st, Jilin was seized. In just a few days, most of the Liaoning and Jilin provinces fell. At that time, the local civil and military officials had no choice but to retreat. This is the main reason why the Northeast was lost. The people had no awareness of the incident beforehand and were not prepared at all. Once the country was lost, the pain was imaginable. However, because they were not prepared, they were also helpless. This is the situation in the first period. Second Period: The second period is from the Jiangqiao Battle to the withdrawal of troops from Jinzhou. After occupying the Liaoning and Jilin provinces, the Japanese further attempted to seize the Heilongjiang provincial capital and Harbin. They believed that without getting these two places, they could not achieve their goal of annexing the Northeast, nor could the puppet state appear on March 1 last year. Therefore, the Japanese resorted to threats against the civil and military officials of Heihe and Harbin, wanting to obtain Heihe and Harbin in the same way as they had seized Liaoning and Jilin. However, the loss of Liaoning and Jilin was because the local civil and military officials did not resist and offered them with both hands, and the people were unprepared and helpless. The situation in Heihe and Harbin was completely different. The people, learning from the loss of Liaoning and Jilin, ran around everywhere, making movements to defend the territory with determination. The most prominent were the provincial and municipal party headquarters and the chambers of commerce, which united to urge the local authorities to resist Japan to the death. Fortunately, General Ma Zhanshan was ordered to act as the chairman of Jiang Province with the title of Heihe Garrison Commander. After arriving in the province, he immediately raised the banner of anti-Japanese resistance and fought with the Japanese. However, when General Ma returned to the province, the provincial treasury was empty, to the point that he did not even have thirty yuan to buy vegetables. The difficulty was imaginable. Because of the support of the people in Heihe and Harbin, the army's supplies gradually became available. However, it was difficult for General Ma to win by collecting troops that were not under his command to resist the Japanese's strong armor and sharp weapons. However, from November 4th to November 20th, half a month of hard fighting caused the Japanese army to suffer thousands of casualties, which the Japanese had not expected when they occupied Liaoning and Jilin. Until Hei Province could not be defended, he retreated to Hailun in order to echo each other with Harbin. After retreating to Hailun, he maintained it until the end of the 20th year. During these two months, the people of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang hoped for one thing, that Jinzhou was still in our hands and that the main forces inside the Pass should be concentrated in Jinzhou as soon as possible. If the Japanese army marched westward, they would fight them to the death. Therefore, the organization of volunteer armies was brewing everywhere to back up the government. The people hoped to accompany the patriotic soldiers who killed the enemy. However, on January 2nd of the 21st year, our army lightly abandoned Jinzhou again. The disappointment of the people in the Northeast can be imagined. However, the strength of the people's anti-Japanese resistance had already surged up. This is the situation in the second period.

Third Period: The third period is from the withdrawal of troops from Jinzhou to General Ma Zhanshan's re-rising to resist Japan. Although the withdrawal of troops from Jinzhou dealt a blow to the people's anti-Japanese movement, the anti-Japanese spirit grew especially strong. Not long after, Harbin fell. On February 5th, the main force of the Japanese army entered Harbin. On March 1st, the puppet state was established. The Japanese further suppressed the people's anti-Japanese forces everywhere with military force, which inevitably suffered some setbacks. This is the situation in the third period.

Fourth Period: The fourth period is from April 3rd of last year, when General Ma Zhanshan escaped from Hei Province and re-rose to resist Japan, to January 2nd of this year, when Shanhaiguan fell. During this period, the people truly fought a bloody battle with the Japanese. The Japanese suffered no less than 20,000 deaths. This situation is not well understood by the outside world, and newspapers have never counted it, because the Chinese side has not investigated, and the Japanese do not announce the truth. Therefore, the outside world does not know the exact number of Japanese casualties. In fact, the minimum is also 20,000 people. This is not a story of propaganda, and solid evidence can be presented. A leader of the Volunteer Army, whose name need not be announced, once used a plan to lure a Japanese brigade to a low-lying place and wiped them out completely, obtaining 2,050 rifles and more than 1,000 iron hats. The head of the brigade commander was cut off with his own saber. Such incidents were not a few. The outside world only knows that there were bitter battles fought by Wang Delin, Feng Zhanhai, Li Haiqing, and other units in the Northeast. In fact, in addition to them, there were many units of 3,000, 5,000, or even 10,000 men scattered throughout the three provinces. Because of inconvenient transportation, they were not well publicized and did not send telegrams, so the outside world knew nothing about it. We also have a piece of evidence, that is, the Japanese never allow the bodies of those killed in battle to be lost. To retrieve a body, they will not hesitate to sacrifice several more people. After retrieving it, they cremate it and put it in a wooden box. A tea servant on the South Manchuria Railway spread the news that from May to September, these wooden boxes were transported back every day, no less than two or three hundred a day. Combining the calculations, saying that the Japanese died 20,000 is actually an underestimate. Because of this reason, the Japanese had no way to deal with the Volunteer Army until the winter of last year. This period was the most active period for the Volunteer Army, and it was also a period that gave Japan a deep and severe blow.

Fifth Period: The fifth period is from the end of last winter to the present. During this period, the situation is very different from before. Ma Su retreated into Russian territory, Feng Li retreated back to Rehe, and part of Wang Delin also retreated to Russian territory. Therefore, the Japanese believe that the Volunteer Army has been wiped out and are concentrating their forces to attack Rehe. However, those who fought hard in the Northeast in the past were not just these few units, but these few units and many other Volunteer Army units jointly resisted Japan. These Volunteer Army units that have not withdrawn from the Northeast are either temporarily lurking or temporarily compromising. There are at least 300,000 people. However, this period is the most critical juncture. If it is done well, the Japanese can be made to be unable to sleep peacefully and be exhausted. Otherwise, not only will the recovery of the Northeast be hopeless, but Rehe and North China will also be difficult to protect, and the whole country will be in great danger. Now, I will talk about them separately.

Three Questions: (1) The Japanese have now driven away the large anti-Japanese troops, and they want to buy off the many small troops with money. Those who do not accept the buy-off will have their guns confiscated. In order to preserve their guns, they have no choice but to compromise with the Japanese temporarily. This compromise is a temporary expedient, which is acceptable. However, if it continues for a long time, the danger will be extremely great, because people are easily accustomed to comfort. Without pain, it is necessary to forget the hatred of national subjugation. Therefore, we should take advantage of the fact that the Japanese have not yet achieved the goal of buying them off and mobilize them to resist Japan permanently. (2) On the Rehe side, if we can resist for three months, the people of the Northeast, even with their bare hands, are willing to fight the Japanese to the death. If we cannot support it for a long time and fail after a resistance, the people of the Northeast will inevitably be disappointed. Therefore, on the one hand, we must actively support Rehe, and on the other hand, we must quickly support the armed comrades who are resisting Japan in the Northeast, so that they know the government's determination to resist. (3) The anti-Japanese resistance of the people in the Northeast is definitely not for the sake of officialdom. There may be a very small number who are for the sake of officialdom. The resistance of the regular army may be for rewards. The resistance of the people is to protect their lives, property, and ancestral graves. Therefore, if the government does not find ways to reward the Volunteer Army who are sacrificing their lives to save the country, the anti-Japanese spirit of the Northeast will gradually decline. These three questions are extremely important. In addition, the lack of contact and guidance among the Northeast Volunteer Army is a local issue that is easy to solve.

Two Examples: In short, the reason why we have to fight with the Japanese now is because the survival of the Northeast is the key to the survival of China. This is not just a slogan, and the evidence is very conclusive. Now I will give two examples: (1) Mr. Huang just mentioned that China's foreign trade had a particularly large deficit last year, totaling 400 million Haikwan taels. Do you know what the reason is? It is because of the loss of the Northeast. In terms of foreign trade volume, China's interior has an annual deficit, while the three northeastern provinces have an annual surplus. The foreign trade volume of the three northeastern provinces accounts for one-third of the country's total. This is in terms of economic lifeline, and the Northeast occupies a very important position. (2) The land in the Northeast has not been fully developed. Every year, millions of people from Hebei, Shandong, and other provinces move to the Northeast. In addition to those who go in the spring and return in the winter, no less than 500,000 people stay in the Northeast every year. The population density in the inland provinces is high, and the Northeast can be used as an overflow. The problem of China's overpopulation can be solved. This is in terms of immigration, and the Northeast occupies a very important position. Furthermore, internationally, both Japan and Russia attach great importance to the Northeast. Even Britain and the United States believe that the Northeast is related to world prosperity and do not want it to be monopolized by Japan. In short, from an economic and international perspective, it is not that the loss of the Northeast has nothing to do with China. It can be said that if the Northeast is lost, China will inevitably be lost, which is not alarmist. Three Conclusions: Based on the situation we have said above, we can draw three conclusions. First, since the September 18th Incident, various parts of the Northeast have continued to fall, so that it is now difficult to clean up. This is not because of insufficient material resources, but because of a too weak mentality. The arms factories in the three northeastern provinces had a large stock of guns, artillery, and ammunition, and there were also more than 200 airplanes. How could the material resources be too bad? However, due to the weak mentality, they retreated again and again. Looking back at the armed forces of the people in the Northeast, with only 100 or 200 bullets for self-defense guns, they were able to resist for a year and a half, which is even more clear. Second, we want to ask whether we should first recover the Northeast and then talk about national revival, or should we first seek revival and then go to recover the Northeast? Our conclusion is that it is difficult for the Chinese nation to revive without first recovering the Northeast. Therefore, we should strive to recover the Northeast first, and then talk about national revival. Third, the anti-Japanese spirit of the people in the Northeast is still enthusiastic, but there is a great danger of being bought off by the Japanese. Therefore, I hope that the people of the whole country, in addition to paying attention to Rehe, will continue to work hard to support the Northeast Volunteer Army, and must make their anti-Japanese spirit and actions continue to grow, and not gradually decline.

National Responsibility: Finally, we recognize the above three conclusions, and we can also get a general conclusion, that is, it is as lucky as the sky if Rehe can be defended for three months. Even if it cannot be defended for three months, we should not be discouraged or disappointed. Once Rehe is lost, we can use the method of supporting and mobilizing the people of the Northeast to also support and mobilize the people of Rehe. In short, for the land that has not been lost, we must fight desperately to resist and defend it. For the land that has been lost, we must never admit that it has been lost and continue to mobilize the people to fight hard. Isn't this a way to deal with the land that has not been lost and a way to deal with the land that has been lost? Finally, there is one more sentence: At the beginning of the establishment of the Northeast Association, I hope that all compatriots in the country can participate and become members of the Northeast Association, because recovering the Northeast and building the Northeast are the responsibility of all compatriots in the country.

Lin Kanghou

Declaration for Saving National Treasury Bonds

A reporter from the National News Agency went to the Bankers' Association yesterday to meet Secretary-General Lin Kanghou and asked him if he had any financial opinions to publish. According to Mr. Lin, he has nothing to express so far. However, in my position and from my standpoint, I am very willing to contribute my opinions that are beneficial to the country to the press. However, there is one important statement. I usually keep my conversations brief, but reporters often add to them in order to fully express their views, which may lead to a loss of their true meaning. For example, a few days ago, someone asked me about saving national treasury bonds. What I said was only that Premier Song had contacted various banks in the north when he was in Peiping and Tianjin, and there should be no problem. However, a certain newspaper reported that there would be a new issuance of public bonds and that the banking industry could bear it. I definitely did not say this and should be corrected. Moreover, I have served in the banking industry for more than ten years and in the Bankers' Association for five or six years. How can I not know the heavy burden of the various banks? This is enough to prove that I did not say the above.

The Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Joint Council was formally established the day before yesterday.
