It is now learned that the council's telegram and exhortation have been issued. The original text is as follows:

Please National Troops Unite to Resist the Enemy (Titles omitted)

Since the violent sun [Japan] invaded, our territory has been lost. The East Province has already fallen, and the Shanghai Incident has just ended. The humiliation has not been avenged, and the blood has not yet dried. Now, they are again losing their minds and committing outrages on our hot border, coveting our Tianjin and Beijing. They disregard international law and abandon humanitarian justice like worn-out shoes, relying on their strong power to escalate the situation. Now, the draft proposal of the Nineteen-Nation Committee has been unanimously passed in the League of Nations, so right and wrong are clear, and justice is obvious. If we do not rise up to resist and fight, we will inevitably place our country in an irrecoverable situation. The crisis is increasingly urgent, and it is unbearable. The only solution is to use armed self-defense. We deeply hope that our national troops will rise up together and swear to defend against aggression to seek survival for the nation, eliminate the barbarian leaders for the world. Success is certainly gratifying, and we can take this opportunity to severely punish the barbarians. Even if we fail, what harm is there? It can also promote the indomitable spirit of our Chinese nation. We citizens see the difficulties of the times and are extremely indignant. We are willing to use our lives and property as a backing for our national anti-Japanese troops, swearing to kill the enemy and share life and death. We present these words with tears, hoping for your kind consideration. The Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Joint Council respectfully salutes you.

Exhortation to Citizens Throughout the District (Titles omitted) Since the violent sun [Japan] invaded and the Northeast fell, Yuguan has been lost, Tianjin and Beijing are shaken, our rivers and mountains are shattered, the copper camels evoke sorrow over the thorns, and the country is in danger. The wheat and millet grieve for the pain of the fallen palace. The surging Black River, the vast Divine Land. Alas, how can our nation not be heartbroken? Now that the government is resisting Japan, it has made a firm decision. Some are engaged in melee combat on the battlefields, while others are volunteering and awaiting orders, with righteousness reaching the heavens. However, once the war starts, it is difficult to end. Military pay, ammunition, and supplies all need to be replenished. Xian Gao saved the country, and Bu Shi contributed his wealth. The spirit of patriotism follows these ancient examples. It is hoped that all citizens will be of one mind, save on food and clothing, and enthusiastically take turns contributing. Do not say that the knife has not yet reached your head and allow yourselves to sit idly by. You must know that the voracious eating and devouring are pressing, and disaster is imminent. Better to be shattered like jade than to be preserved like tile. This is the time! This council sees that the country's demise is imminent and feels that silence is difficult to bear. Loving our country, we dare not lag behind. Relying on the strength of the masses to save the nation, we are determined to be the vanguard of all citizens, encouraging the three armies and boosting our morale, to eliminate the fierce and stubborn and secure our national borders. May our citizens truly benefit the country. (Same name as above)

Youth Association Plans Service in War Zone 89

The National Association of the Chinese Christian Youth Association, in view of the increasingly tense war in Rehe, and the large number of troops gathering in Rehe, there are many areas where spiritual and material services are needed.

Such as the transportation of comfort items, the transportation of medicine, the improvement of diet, the provision of military camp sanitation, the need for entertainment, the need for recreational items, etc., the Youth Association, based on its principle of serving youth, has unanimously passed at the board meeting on February 28, the principle of the National Youth Association engaging in non-combat war zone service, and will establish the Chinese Christian Youth Association National War Service Committee, (abbreviated as "Youth Association War Committee",) to direct thirty-nine cities nationwide.

The Youth Association and one hundred school Youth Association war zone service matters. The Ministry of Industry now presents the general outline of its war zone service plan, extracted as follows. Based on the Chinese Youth Association's war zone service among Chinese laborers in France during the European War, there are the following items: (1) Collection and distribution of comfort items, (2) Comforting wounded soldiers and writing letters home on their behalf, (3) Cooperating with the Red Cross to collect and supply medicines and first aid supplies, (4) Establishing rest stops for soldiers on major roads, providing tea and refreshments to passing troops, (5) Establishing bathhouses, barbershops, entertainment rooms, and implementing other educational works in fixed locations, (6) Recruiting and training rescue personnel for agencies engaged in rescuing wounded soldiers, (7) Supplying soldiers with books and newspapers. Currently, the Youth Association has dispatched Dr. Nan Bingfang and Mr. Ai Dexu to the front lines of Beijing, Tianjin, and Rehe to investigate the actual situation and contact the responsible officials. Furthermore, Zhang Jiafu, Chen Xiangtao, Chen Liting, Zhu Lide, Kuang Fuzhuo, Hao Boyang, Li Daonan, Li Yaobang, Liu Zhanen, Li Zhaohuan, Bao Huigen, Shen Siliang, Cao Yunxiang, and Zhao Jinqing have been appointed as the reporting committee members of the Youth Association War Committee. It is reported that the committee will hold a meeting at 12:00 noon on March 4 at the Bank Association, etc.

Shipping Representatives Go to the Capital 92

To Petition for the Amendment of the Maritime Law

The Shanghai shipping industry, because the Legislative Yuan passed the Maritime Law, Article 23 of which contains provisions that are very unfavorable to shipping companies and are practically impossible to implement, has publicly elected representatives to go to the capital to petition for amendments. The general situation is recorded as follows:

The provisions are improper. Shanghai shipping companies believe that Article 33 of the promulgated Maritime Law stipulates that if a sunken merchant ship obstructs navigation, the customs authorities may carry out salvage or demolition if they deem it necessary, and all costs shall still be borne by the shipowner. They believe this is inappropriate and practically difficult to implement. A similar incident occurred last year, causing major difficulties.

Repeated requests for amendments. After the Dachang ship was sunk by the Dahua ship last year, the customs authorities notified the Dachang shipowner, limiting them to salvage the ship, otherwise the customs authorities would carry out the salvage at the expense of the shipowner. At that time, it was estimated that the cost of salvaging the ship would be tens of thousands of yuan. The Dachang shipowner did not want to salvage it again and reported it to the Shipping Association. After discussion, it was decided that after the shipowner abandoned the salvage rights, the costs of salvaging or demolishing the ship, if the customs authorities deemed it necessary, should be borne by the government. Because shipping companies have already paid tonnage dues, the customs authorities should be responsible for maintaining navigation routes, and the shipowners should not be responsible for the salvage costs. The Shipping Association has repeatedly contacted the Ministry of Transportation and the Ministry of Finance to request corrections to this provision, but has not yet received any results.

Representatives go to the capital. Shanghai shipping companies believe that it cannot be delayed any longer, so the Shipping Association held a meeting to discuss and decided to send three representatives to the capital to petition. Chen Bogang (Executive Committee Member of the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association), Chen Shuntong (General Manager of the Zhongwei Shipping Company, a senior figure in the shipping industry), and Wei Wenhan (Legal Advisor to the Shipping Association) were elected to represent the entire industry in the city and went to the capital yesterday morning to petition for amendments.

Request for corrections. Chen Bogang, Chen Shuntong, and others, entrusted with the important task of representing all Shanghai shipping companies, went to the Ministry of Transportation in the capital to meet with Minister Zhu Jia骅 to explain the facts and reasons why Article 23 of the Maritime Law was difficult to implement, and to present their opinions on the amendments that should be made, requesting Minister Zhu to accommodate the opinions of all shipping companies and submit Article 23 to the Legislative Yuan for re-amendment. The three representatives are currently petitioning in the capital.

National Economic Council Plans to Build Highways in Seven Provinces 93

Convenes a Specialist Meeting to Determine Routes

To be Completed by the End of This Year

Sends League of Nations Advisor to Assist Jiangxi in Road Construction

In order to expedite transportation and facilitate bandit suppression, the central government is actively planning to build highways in various provinces. Chairman Jiang and Minister Song are paying particular attention to this. They previously engaged in a large-scale plan to build connecting highways in the seven provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Hunan. The National Economic Council is urging the provinces to implement the plan. The total length of the routes is over 20,000 kilometers, requiring over 100 million yuan. Minister Song, recognizing the provinces' insufficient financial resources, is allocating significant funds from the central government to provide continuous assistance. The construction methods are being carried out in phases, depending on the urgency of the situation and the financial strength of each region.

Expanding to seven provinces. It is reported that since receiving the order, the council has first focused on the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, and is working closely with the construction authorities in each province. The highways in the three provinces that were completed in October last year include the entire Shanghai-Hangzhou Road, as well as parts of the Hangzhou-Huizhou, Suzhou-Jiaxing, Xuanjing, and Wuhu roads. Since Chairman Jiang convened a highway conference in the seven provinces in Hankou, the first phase of highway construction in the seven provinces was set to a total length of approximately 1,600 kilometers. In Henan Province, there are the routes from Zhang Laorenbu to Huangchuan, Shuangliushu to Xiaojieling, Zhou Dangban to Xuandian, and Guangshan to Jingfu. In Hubei Province, there are the routes from Xiaojieling to Wuxue, Susong to Qishui, Luotian to Yingshan, and Tianjiazhen to Qishui. In Anhui Province, there are the routes from Ningguo to Shexian, Shexian to Yulingguan, Wangniudun to Langxi, Langxi to Shilipu, Xuancheng to Jiepai, and Yingshan to Taihu. In Jiangsu Province, there is the route from Nanjing to Wangniudun. In Zhejiang Province, there are the routes from Changhua to Yulingguan and Xiasi'an to Jiepai. In Jiangxi Province, there is the route from Yujiang to Guangfeng. The construction of the above routes has started one after another, and all provinces are enthusiastically engaged in the work, with the completion deadline not far off.

Specialist meeting. Recently, in order to promote the implementation plan, the council convened a specialist committee meeting on highways in the seven provinces. Concrete regulations were also made for the routes to be built in the second phase, with a total length of approximately 6,000 kilometers, to be completed by the end of December this year. The important meetings and key bandit areas in the seven provinces are generally passed by the routes in this phase. In addition to those built by the provinces, there are also those designated by Chairman Jiang to be built by the military.

Increasing highway construction. The main routes in Henan Province are Yejiaji to Zhang Laorenbu, Hanchuan to Xinyang, Xiangcheng to Hanchuan, Luoyang to Linru, and Yongcheng to Shangqiu. The main routes in Hubei Province are Shahan to Yichang and Laohekou to Mengjialou. The main routes in Anhui Province are from Wujiang via Hexian, Chaoxian, Hefei, and Liuan to Yejiaji, and Hefei to Anqing. The main routes in Jiangxi Province are Linchuan to Yongfeng, Jingdezhen to Huangjinbu, Ji'an to Chaling, and Shanggao to Liuyang. The main routes in Jiangsu Province are Zhenjiang to Shanghai, Pukou to Jiangtian, Pukou to Wujiang, Suqian to Muyang, and Taierzhuang. The main routes in Zhejiang Province are Cao'e to Shengxian, Xinchang to Linhai, Fuyang to Jiangshan, and Jinhua to Yongjia. The main routes in Hunan Province are Liuyang to Wanzai, Liuyang to Yong'an City, Baji to Yongxin, Fengxian to Changde, and Taohuaping to Huitong. It is expected that if all of this phase is completed, the connection between the capital and the cities of the seven provinces can be directly reached without obstruction.

Unified planning. It is reported that in addition to the route plan, the meeting also included unified planning for the naming, numbering, mileage signs, mutual communication of automobiles and long-distance buses, investigation and registration of technical personnel, search and research of road-building materials and automobile fuels, and various technical and administrative matters related to highways. They will be gradually implemented. In addition, due to the bandit suppression situation in Jiangxi recently, road construction is the most tense. The council has recently received a telegram from Chairman Jiang and has sent League of Nations advisors and engineers to urge and assist. It has also tried to allocate and borrow as much as possible road-building tools, such as iron rails and dump trucks.

After Stopping Participation in the Chicago Expo, Exhibitors Decide to Participate on Their Own 94

Meeting to Discuss This Afternoon

Preparatory Committee Meeting Resolves to End

Since the Executive Yuan decided to stop China's participation in the Chicago Expo, the Preparatory Committee specially convened an emergency meeting yesterday to discuss how to end the preparations. The exhibitors also sent representatives to attend and participate. It was immediately resolved that the Preparatory Committee would end its work immediately, but the exhibitors would organize an association to go to the United States to participate and hold an exhibition of the items collected. Yesterday, many people still visited the collection exhibition. The Review Committee has completed the review of all the collected items. The details are divided into the following sections: Preparatory Committee Convenes Emergency Meeting

The Preparatory Committee convened a meeting in the conference room of the International Trade Bureau at 3:00 PM yesterday. The attending committee members included Cai Wuji, Zou Bingwen, Xu Xinliu, Zhang Yichou, Xu Shanxiang, He Bingxian, Guo Bingwen, and Yu Kaizhan. The observers included Miao Zhongxiu, Guo Weibai, and Zhang Xianghe. The exhibitor side also sent Zhou Guanhong, Dong Kunfan, and Wang Zhengji to attend the meeting. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. After the meeting, He Bingxian stated that the resolutions could be divided into three points: (1) He would be responsible for returning all the collected items immediately. (2) The collection office would be in charge of the conference affairs, administration, and publicity, with the assistance of the three offices. (3) The Review Committee would continue to review and grade the items to award prizes. The rest was not convenient to be released.

Exhibitors Decide to Participate on Their Own

After the meeting, Zhou Guanhong and other exhibitor representatives who attended the meeting told the National News Agency reporters that although the central government decided to stop participation due to the deepening national crisis, all the exhibits have been collected and are ready, and the public opinion in all circles is extremely praised. The enthusiasm of the exhibitors is particularly enthusiastic. It would be a pity to stop it rashly. Therefore, it was decided that the exhibitors would organize an association to participate on their own, not in the name of the country. The Preparatory Committee has no objection to this move. It has been decided to convene a meeting of all exhibitors at the venue at 2:00 PM this afternoon to discuss the methods. The name will be tentatively set as "Republic of China Chicago Expo Exhibitor Association."

All Collected Items Reviewed

The collection exhibition is scheduled to close on the 5th as originally planned. Now that the closing date is approaching, many people still visited yesterday. As for the Review Committee, it was originally scheduled to complete the review on March 2. Therefore, the Review Committee completed the review of all the exhibits as scheduled yesterday and has submitted the report to the Collection Exhibition. It is temporarily divided into two types: qualified and unqualified. It is reported that in the future, if the exhibits do not go to the United States, they will be graded again, and the Review Committee of each group will decide on the award. It is also learned that the Collection Exhibition has now been prepared by the General Affairs Director Xu Binhua to compile a report, the content of which is the various circumstances of this conference, in order to distribute it to all circles for memory.

But if we have such fearless troops, and can provide them with the modern weaponry of war, what worries are there that we will not be victorious in every battle? Therefore, the people of our country, with Shanghai as the focus of national attention, hope that you will help, make every effort to proceed, and make Shanghai's success the guiding light for national success." After the speech, the group discussed the methods for each team to carry out recruitment, and the meeting adjourned at 5:50 PM.

Each Team Recruits Staff

The captains of each recruitment team were out yesterday recruiting staff, extremely busy. The results were also very satisfactory. It is expected that the list of team members for each team will be announced soon. Team captains continued to come to collect membership application forms in an endless stream. Huang Boqiao, the director of both the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, took away 5,000 copies. Li Ting'an, the director of the Municipal Health Bureau, took away 5,000 copies. Wu Shanjun of the Roads Association took away 6,000 copies. Zheng Zenan, the chief of the Fourth Tunnel, took away 5,000 copies. It is also heard that each team has convened team meetings to discuss various organized methods. Some advocate taking occupation or organization as a unit, recruiting all people in these occupations and organizations as members of the Aviation Association. If each organization follows this approach, then all citizens of the city, except the unemployed, can be recruited as members.

Children's Day Fees Proposed to Supplement Donations

Fang Debao and Fang Demin, two brothers who are students at the Huahua Middle School on Yuyuan Road, having witnessed the destruction caused by Japanese aircraft in Shanghai last year, and the current bombing of the Rehe people by Japanese aircraft, and recognizing the weakness of our country's air force, which cannot resist the attacks, have bravely initiated the donation of funds for the purchase of a "Children's" aircraft. They urged children to save their candy money and offer it as donations. Children from all teams are also enthusiastically contributing. Today (the 2nd), Fang Debao brought a donation of 270 yuan to the office of the recruitment team of the Aviation Association at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA and paid the full amount. Their patriotic enthusiasm is truly commendable.

Chinese and Western Doctors Donate One Day's Income

Li Ting'an, the captain of the 274th team of the Shanghai Municipal Chapter of the China Aviation Association, and the current director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, in order to expand the recruitment work, sent letters to his close friends and figures in the medical and pharmaceutical fields and health experts, inviting them to a meeting at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA at 8:00 PM the day before yesterday to discuss recruitment plans. After Captain Li presented the proposal, it was unanimously approved with applause. The meeting adjourned at about 1:00 AM.

National Customs Officials Donate Over 300,000

According to reliable sources yesterday, national customs officials have now collected donations of approximately 300,000 yuan, which will be remitted to Nanjing within days to purchase aircraft for the purpose of resisting Japan. However, this donation is unrelated to the regular, long-term donation of 5% of monthly salary previously initiated by the customs authorities. The long-term donation is limited to Chinese officials in each customs office, while this large donation was collected from all customs personnel. In addition, it is understood that the long-term donations from Chinese customs officials for February, the first month of the donation period, totaled 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. Combining the two items above, the customs authorities have donated a total of over 350,000 yuan.

County Government Allocates a Percentage of Salary to Assist Donations

The Shanghai County Government received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs stating that, due to the urgency of foreign aggression, the entire country should unite to support national defense. Aviation aircraft are especially needed. It has been determined that public officials will contribute according to a graded percentage of their salaries. Please comply accordingly. Upon receiving the order, Magistrate Yan issued instructions yesterday that, starting with the February salary, from the magistrate to the staff, all will donate according to the percentage. The money will be remitted to the Department of Civil Affairs. This will be done monthly from now on.

Addicted to Gambling, He Actually Died 96

Shi Xingen, Alias, Dies by Poison

Blame Yourself, Yet Pitiable

Shi Xingen, a native of Ningbo, 36 years old, worked as a shop assistant at a German-owned beef noodle shop at 79 Rue du Consulat. However, because Shi had a penchant for gambling, his wages were never enough to cover his spending, and he was heavily in debt. A week ago, he borrowed a fur coat from his colleague, Shen Zhanglong, and sold it for 26 yuan, but unfortunately, he lost that in gambling as well. Unable to return to the shop, he became filled with resentment the day before yesterday and conceived the idea of ending his life. Alone, he went to the Kai Lai Inn at 1 Hubei Road, under the alias Lin Shifa, and attempted suicide by opium smoking. The next morning, the inn's tea boy, Wang Atang, caught sight of him moaning in bed and realized something was wrong. He immediately reported it to the accounting office, who sent him to Huiji Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. The hospital reported it to the Lao Zha Police Station, who ordered detective Peng Yutang to investigate. They found a note next to the deceased with the address of his friend Yan Abao. The detective went to his friend's address and learned that his real name was Shi Xingen. The body was taken to the Forensic Examination Office on Faelan Road. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court commissioned Prosecutor Guo Wei to come to the office to examine the body. After confirming the body, the court questioned Yan Abao, who stated that the deceased was his colleague and that his parents were in his hometown. He had borrowed over a hundred yuan from him. He felt sorry for him and had bought a coffin for him, requesting to claim the body. He also recounted the previous events. Prosecutor Guo then confirmed that the deceased Lin Shifa was indeed Shi Xingen, and that he had died of opium poisoning. The body was released to Yan Abao with a written guarantee to claim the body for burial.

Empty Coffin Summons Spirit 98

丨The incident caused a sensation in the neighborhood due to superstition丨

Xu Fu, a native of Jiangyin, lives at 21 Dongchang Lane, Lan Ni Du, Pudong. He has a wife and a concubine, and their lives are prosperous. Xu's concubine, Ms. Lin, is quite superstitious. It was recently rumored that her brother, Mr. Lin, had taken a position on a certain ship, which encountered an accident near Qingdao. Ms. Xu, upon hearing the news, cried uncontrollably and felt restless. She repeatedly sought divination, which indicated that the prospects were more ominous than auspicious. Ms. Xu Lin became even more mentally disturbed. The day before yesterday, she secretly went to Yangjiadu to purchase a coffin and hired workers to carry the empty coffin to a temporary resting place in the wasteland near Xu's residence, intending to bury it. According to Ms. Xu Lin, it was a coffin for summoning her brother's spirit for burial. The neighbors all found it strange, and the news spread throughout Pudong. The matter came to the attention of Zhang Mingqin, the district chief of the Third District, who, given the current unstable situation, feared that bad people might have other intentions. He sent district officer Cai Zanzhou, along with detectives and deputy team leaders, to investigate. After confirming that it was an empty coffin, they went to the residence of the person involved to question Ms. Xu Lin about the truth. Only then did they learn the story. However, the Xu family had no prior knowledge of the matter until the police district sent officers to investigate. Later, Xu reprimanded Ms. Xu Lin for the superstitious act.

China National Aviation Corporation Announces Chartered Flight Tour Arrangements 100

Air Travel Available at Any Time

China National Aviation Corporation's newly opened aerial tours and aerial trips to Suzhou and Hangzhou are ready, and chartered flight arrangements have also been made, allowing for landings at will. In the midst of this aviation movement, it is also a method of promotion. The details are as follows:

Aerial Tours Available at Any Time

According to Mr. Cai of the company's sales department, the company's aerial tours are available for passengers at any time. There is no such thing as a stop or start. However, as it is now winter, and the cold is severe, naturally no one wants to spend money on an aerial tour. Therefore, in winter, it naturally enters a state of suspension. Now that spring has returned, anyone who wants to ride can do so at any time. As long as they can gather four people and pay 50 yuan, they can fly for 15 minutes.

Newly Chartered Flights Can Land at Will

As for aerial trips to Suzhou and Hangzhou, general passengers regret that they cannot land, otherwise they could take a tour of scenic areas. However, this regret is due to fixed rules that cannot be resolved. Therefore, new chartered flight arrangements have now been made, which can be directed by passengers and land at any time. The prices are divided into several types: (1) The Lockheed aircraft can seat five people, costing 250 yuan per hour. The Stinson aircraft can seat only four people, costing 200 yuan per hour. The minimum time for both is one hour. They are now available for rent. Those who wish to charter them can go to make reservations.

The Sand Junk's Voyage Around the World 102

The New Horizon Encounters Danger Mid-Voyage

After Two Days at Sea, It Travels Eighty Miles and the Main Mast is Broken by a Strong Wind

It is Now Returning to Shanghai for Repairs and Is Scheduled to Make a Second Voyage North Next Sunday

The Shanghai Times reports that the sand junk New Horizon sailed out of Shanghai, intending to make a voyage around the world. Unexpectedly, after only two days at sea, traveling about eighty miles, a strong wind on Thursday night of last week broke the main mast. The huge sail was lowered as a result. It was dark, and the waves were raging. The crew members all looked at each other in dismay. The ship drifted and eventually ran aground on a mudflat. The rudder was also broken. Therefore, the crew decided to return to Shanghai for repairs. It arrived in port on Sunday night, but the crew was not discouraged. The lower spar has now been replaced with sturdier wood, and other parts of the ship have also been repaired. It is now scheduled to depart for the second time next Sunday.

Sand Junk Ship Owners Request Oil Tax Exemption 103

A Petition Submitted Months Ago Has Been Shelved by the Executive Yuan Without Approval

Since the operation of sand junk shipping, the business of sand junk merchants has been declining, almost to the point of being as rare as morning stars. Those who are still able to maintain it are fully supported by the lower tax rate for sand junk shipping and the abolition of the likin tax, which allows them to barely maintain the livelihood of the ship owners. Since the September 18th Incident, with the blockade of the Northeast, the customs has classified soybean oil as a foreign good, increasing the tax rate to 12.5%, causing panic among general shipping merchants and ship owners. They are concerned that the soybean cake and soybeans of the same industry are still tax-exempt as principal goods, while soybean oil has been reclassified as a foreign good and is subject to heavy taxes, which has a huge impact, especially since sand junks have always specialized in transporting soybean oil. Their suffering is immense, and the livelihood of shipping merchants and ship owners is almost cut off. Repeated requests to various superiors have been shelved without approval, and letters have gone unanswered, causing general shipping merchants and ship owners to look forward every day. Zhang Xueliang carried the victory north, and all seaports have thawed. They plan to convene a meeting of fellow tradesmen to discuss and appeal to various agencies, and to contact relevant industry associations to work together, hoping that the strength of the joint efforts will arouse the attention of the authorities.

Qiu Changsheng Is Accused of Plotting to Seize Inheritance 104

He Was Summoned Again by the Court Yesterday

Both Sides Are Very Close to a Settlement

But a Contract Has Not Yet Been Signed

The Plaintiff Hopes for a Quick Resolution

Qiu Changsheng, residing at 184 Tongren Road, is the adopted son of the late Shanghai businessman Qiu Weiqing. Recently, due to plotting to seize the inheritance, his stepmother, Madam Qiu Sun, through her lawyers Zheng and Kai, filed a complaint with the First Court, accusing him of violating Articles 363 and 365 of the Criminal Code. The prosecution's arguments were briefly: (1) The defendant was originally the son of the Jiang family. Recently, there was even a letter from his biological mother requesting his return to his family. This was well known by the clan members since he was raised. Therefore, during the compilation of the genealogy in the past, it was indicated that he was an adopted son. The defendant, knowing that this was inappropriate, sold it and had another one engraved, and bought the original genealogy. (2) The late Qiu Weiqing had instructed the plaintiff to raise his own son, Changyin, and daughter, Shuying. At the time of his death, he left instructions to take good care of them, and because the plaintiff was a woman and knew that Changsheng was the most unreliable, he ordered his nephew Qiu Sheng'er to manage the property, stating that it must be returned only when the children came of age. He had a will. However, the defendant induced Madame Zhu Qiu and the late Qiu Jia to jointly file a lawsuit against Qiu Sheng'er in court, resulting in the defendant actually controlling everything. (3) The late husband's estate should be inherited by his biological children and the plaintiff, but the defendant is only an adopted son and can only be given a small portion. He actually distributed 45% of the estate to himself, which is why the clan leader Qiu Hengzhi and others refused to sign the division. However, the defendant still took decisive measures and seized it by force. (4) Since Qiu Changsheng is an adopted son, he has no mother-son relationship with the plaintiff. After the death of the late husband, he showed no respect for his elders. Last winter, in order to temporarily avoid his bad treatment, she requested funds from Changsheng to go to Hangzhou for medical treatment. Changsheng initially refused to give it to her, but eventually forced her to sign a receipt. At that time, she was critically ill and could not afford to delay treatment. What does she care about signing the receipt? Forcing his mother to sign a receipt is truly contemptible. After toiling hard with the late husband for 60 years, she has what she has today, but after the husband's death, she is forced to leave by her adopted son. Is there such a thing in the world? (5) On March 4th of this year, Madame Jia died. The defendant immediately plotted to open the iron safe without permission. After much reasoning, the case was reported to the police station, and patrolman Chen Jiting was dispatched to the scene. He guarded it for more than ten days to prevent her from being completely occupied. (6) The residence on Tongfu Road was originally divided and belongs to Changjiu. However, the defendant still occupies it and refuses to return it. He also set up iron bars inside the residence, as if facing a major enemy. It can be imagined that he has an unfavorable heart for the children. Since the court has summoned him several times, the defendant has not appeared. His agent told the court that a settlement was possible and postponed the hearing until yesterday afternoon. The plaintiff's lawyer, Zheng Kai, stated that the delay has continued until now. Recently, they have tried to negotiate a settlement, but a contract has not yet been signed. Therefore, the appellant requested that the shortest possible date be set, even two or three days, in order to handle it. If a settlement can be reached, he will submit a statement withdrawing the claim. The judge, Wen Huan, approved the request and postponed the hearing.

Jianghai Customs Issues Notice on Revised Paper Goods Tax Rates 105

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Lofland, Customs Commissioner, issued Notice No. 1278 yesterday, stating that in accordance with government orders, the tax rates for top-grade, second-grade, and third-grade paper in the re-export tariff will be suspended from February 27th of this year as follows: Top-grade paper, valued at over 12 taels of Kaiping silver per picul, will be taxed at 7 mace of Customs silver (including coarse paper and family ledgers; newly published Chinese books and newspapers are exempt from tax). Second-grade paper, valued at over 11 taels of Customs silver per picul, will be taxed at 4 mace of Customs silver. Third-grade paper, valued at 6 taels of Customs silver per picul or more, will be taxed at 2 mace of Customs silver. There are no changes to the tax rates for other paper goods. Merchants are hereby notified.

The Public Concession Bureau Reorganizes House Numbers 106

Twenty-Two Roads

Reorganized on April 1st

The North China Daily News reported that the Public Concession Bureau is reorganizing the house numbers within the concession. This work will sweep away the chaotic state of the house numbers and will be welcomed by all residents of Shanghai. To date, after three years of work, 75 roads have had all street-facing and lane-facing houses reorganized with new house numbers. This year, it is planned to reorganize 22 roads starting on April 1st. According to the Public Concession Bureau, this initiative was originally launched in 1930, and a special committee was organized to discuss it. The committee then recommended a new method of numbering houses. Roads with an absolute need for house number reorganization were prioritized, followed by others in sequence, in order to reduce temporary inconveniences for residents. The Public Concession Bureau then decided to gradually implement this new system throughout the entire concession. However, due to the large number of roads and lanes within the concession and the complexity of the procedures, it cannot be completed in a short period of time. But once this numbering is completed, it can be used permanently. The numbering method is no longer based on the number of houses. Every twelve feet along the road is numbered, with even and odd numbers on the left and right sides of the road. Lane entrances are numbered the same as the adjacent houses, and houses within the lane are numbered separately. Therefore, even if houses are rebuilt in the future, there is no need to change the house numbers.

"L> Special Education News

"P> Ideal Rural Education (Part 2)

(1) Clearly define the purpose and implementation guidelines of rural education; (2) Increase funding for rural education, and reward talents who handle rural education; (3) Rural Education Department In-Service Training Seminar during the winter vacation; (4) Merge ordinary unsuitable level elementary schools, plan compulsory education areas, and reallocate school locations (sponsored by the education bureaus of various counties); (5) Separately print textbooks suitable for rural elementary schools; (6) Normal schools pay attention to practical rural education lectures and internships; (7) Implement rural social education effectively;

Comment

We cannot bear to see the country perpetually trapped in a semi-colonial state and constantly divided, so we feel that transforming rural education is the most urgent matter. However, this is not just talk; it requires consistent effort from top to bottom. Simply relying on the rural education, not only is there no education to speak of, but it is also very easy to cause trouble. Education can save the country, but it can also harm the country, or even destroy it. How can China's rural education not be disheartening?

Last month, I returned to my hometown on business and took the opportunity to observe the so-called expanded compulsory education. The rural education in my hometown [Jiangyin], which ranked second in Jiangsu Province, is unbearable. The rural elementary schools there are shocking. Reasonable education is that of the Former Han Dynasty, but a few years ago, an elementary school in my hometown with one or two hundred students now only has thirty or forty. Private schools are everywhere, and farmers have no respect for schools. Although there are various reasons for this, the fact that expenses have been in arrears for as long as eight months is also a major reason for the bankruptcy of rural education. This is the entire problem of rural education, and I urge the authorities to pay special attention to it. Japan, Italy, and Turkey's revitalization can be used as a lesson. They all relied on the power of education, especially elementary school education. Small countries occupy more than 80% of the national rural education. Why neglect it? Finally, I silently wish that everyone will work hard on rural education, so that all my ideals will become a reality in the shortest possible time.

"P> Zhejiang Education Department Promotes Production Education

Promulgation of Implementation Plan for Affiliated Elementary Schools of Provincial Middle Schools

丨Seven Items Including Sub-Goals, Equipment, and Environment

丨Practical, Concrete, Easy to Implement Teaching

丨Progress Limited to Reporting and Verification This Semester

The Zhejiang Education Department, based on the resolution of this year's Provincial Middle School Affiliated Elementary School Conference, "Please ask the Provincial Education Department to formulate and issue a production education implementation plan to each affiliated elementary school as the basis for education," stated that the reason for our country's lies in the underdevelopment of agriculture, commerce, and industry. Land cannot be fully utilized, and resources cannot be fully used. The biggest reason is that there are few producers and many consumers. In order to actively relieve the current social danger, it is necessary to promote production education as the foundation of construction. The association's views were insightful and were approved by the directive. The Education Department has specially formulated a production education implementation plan for affiliated elementary schools of provincial middle schools and ordered it to be issued to provincial senior middle schools and other schools to instruct affiliated elementary schools to refer to it for implementation, and the progress of the implementation should be recorded in the "New Facilities" column of the school affairs report form at the end of the semester for assessment.

Zhejiang Provincial Middle School Affiliated Elementary School Production Education Implementation Plan

(1) Determine Goals

The implementation of production education in affiliated elementary schools of provincial middle schools is based on the overall goals of elementary education as determined by the Ministry of Education. The overall goals of elementary education are: Elementary schools should develop children's physical and mental health based on the Three Principles of the People, in accordance with the educational purpose of the Republic of China and its implementation guidelines, cultivate national morals, provide basic knowledge and skills necessary for life, so as to cultivate civilized and patriotic citizens. The analysis is as follows: (1) Cultivate children's healthy physique, (2) Cultivate children's good character, (3) Develop children's aesthetic interests, (4) Increase children's knowledge of life, (5) Train children's labor habits, (6) Inspire children's scientific thinking, (7) Cultivate children's spirit of mutual assistance and unity, (8) Cultivate children's concept of patriotism.

(2) Increase Equipment

(1) In addition to sports fields and ordinary study rooms, it is best to set up a farm, factory, pasture, cooking room, sewing room, and cooperative to give children extensive opportunities to practice productive industries. Otherwise, school gardens, workshops, animal breeding centers, home practice rooms, and small shops should be considered the minimum equipment standards for affiliated elementary schools to implement production education. (2) In addition to the existing equipment for each subject, sufficient equipment should be prepared for natural experiments and all labor education tools to enhance teaching effectiveness. (3) Simple experimental equipment, ordinary animal and plant specimens and models should be used to guide children to make them themselves (i.e., achieve the purpose of knowing through the means of doing). Ordinary mineral specimens should be used to guide children to collect them themselves, and models should be provided to show the entire process. The principle (for example, the coal specimen should not be just a few lumps of coal. The mining, coal seam excavation, and transportation methods should be displayed together to show the entire process). (4) It is best to set up similar machines to enable children to make daily utensils, repair daily appliances, and practice a stable skill as the basis for life, which is the best way for affiliated elementary schools to expand their facilities.

(3) Utilize

The production of the school itself is different depending on the environment. For example, using mountains forests, using fields, cultivating plants, using paddy fields, planting rice and wheat, using to raise, utilizing adjacent open spaces to plant cotton, vegetables, seedlings, sugarcane, corn, and potatoes, utilizing ponds, planting to raise fish, using farms to raise bees, raising rabbits, and sheep and pigs, utilizing workbenches, printing binding books, painting appliances, manufacturing children's items, game equipment, and daily household goods, utilizing home practice rooms, manufacturing school notebooks, clothes, and Students, refreshments, and other cooperative operations such as shop, food and clothing consumption cooperation, research and improvement of local specialties must be integrated with production education teaching at any time and place, so that children in a pure and natural environment have the opportunity to experience their own simple economic life.

(4) Pay Attention to Labor Training

Labor without production is like filling hunger with paintings, and production without labor is like quenching thirst with plums. Therefore, labor depends on production, and production is driven by labor. The scope of labor is defined as follows: (1) In terms of agriculture, it is divided into gardening, farming, and breeding; (2) In terms of factories, it is divided into specialty crafts (such as Huzhou's silk and Ningbo's mats, etc.) and weaving, carpentry, earthwork, and gold work, five types (senior students can specialize in one or two types); (3) In terms of health, it is divided into and relief, and disaster relief two types; (4) Practical operation, refers to various operations attached to the living environment and career, roughly as follows: (1) Cleaning includes movements such as drawing, washing, and beating; (2) Transportation includes movements such as loading, pulling, and rowing; (3) Construction includes movements such as excavation, stacking, throwing, and catching; (4) Agriculture includes movements such as reaping, stepping, and trampling; (5) Crafts include movements such as chopping, sawing, and weaving; (6) Fire fighting includes movements such as climbing, running, and long-distance running; (7) includes movements such as mixing, supporting, and carrying; (8) Others include operations in language, arithmetic, social studies, natural science, and all hand-brain combined movements that have educational meaning.

For the above items, children should be guided to learn from various activities according to their abilities, interests, and actual needs, and to transform children who are rich in imitative and malleable qualities into small farmers and small workers, actively and joyfully. From this activity, do not use labor as hard work. In addition to "appreciation" and "research," pay attention to avoiding waste, maintaining order, cultivating mutual assistance, increasing production efficiency, and developing a positive attitude and creativity.

(5) Improve Teaching Methods

(1) The curriculum standards should be based on the Ministry of Education's elementary school curriculum standards and the local special environment, refined teaching materials, and adapted to children's needs; (2) The curriculum standards should be based on the Ministry of Education's general rules for elementary school education, and each subject should be taught with the key teaching principles of "using both hands and brain," "practicing what you preach," and ""; (3) The teaching materials for natural, social, labor, art, and hygiene subjects must have appropriate organized connections and be designed and taught in large units to break the previous rigid teaching, standard experiments, and interesting practice, so that children can actually participate in the real environment of life, society, and labor around them. In addition to observing with their own eyes, listening with their own ears, and experiencing in person, they must also do it with their own hands. Not only should they do what can be done in labor class, but also what cannot be done in labor class, they should fully try to do it during class time or outside of class time. If there are observation, research, and experimental matters that must go through a long period of time before results can be obtained, children should be guided to do them every day and record the progress every day until there are results to report. (4) Each teacher should provide appropriate guidance and inspection for the work done by children.

(6) Promote Guidance on Further Education and Employment

(1) Each affiliated elementary school should organize a guidance committee for further education and employment, and each teacher should be responsible for group observation, conduct intelligence tests, performance tests, and investigations of family environment and personal aspirations to guide children in further education or employment. (2) Each affiliated elementary school should jointly organize a job placement agency with social education institutions and professional groups to select employment paths for graduates and reduce the hesitation in choosing a career.

(7) Concurrently Conduct Mass Education

(1) Each affiliated elementary school should hold production education symposiums regularly, inviting students' parents, siblings, and neighbors to attend. In addition to lecturing on matters related to production, they may also exhibit or perform on the achievements of production education. (2) Each affiliated elementary school should take its own children as the center and promote children's and youth production competitions in the local area (such as chicken competitions, egg incubation competitions, fruit and vegetable planting competitions, etc.). (3) Help society destroy enemies and destroy , eliminate borers and locusts, introduce new agricultural tools, irrigate and instill scientific knowledge, compile specific measures, guide children to help their fathers and brothers in production and employment during holidays, and conduct performance assessments. (4) Each affiliated elementary school may set up women's vocational tutoring classes to directly improve people's livelihoods and indirectly increase children's happiness. (5) Plan to establish a mobile library on aspects of the people's livelihood. (6) Use spare time on Sundays to carry out oral or written propaganda on aspects of the people's livelihood.

"L> Reader Consultant

"P> The Burden of Children

丨A letter from Mr. Fahua in this city

After reading your article "Is My Suicide View Right or Wrong?" in response to Mr. Ren Wangyue, I feel very satisfied. Although I have never thought about suicide, the you gave him are very correct!

Now I have a problem that has been unresolved for many years, and I hope you will give me a good guide as well.

I have been married for four years. My husband and I do not have the intense love that young men and women have these days, but we both have the will to stand in the ranks of the common people and overthrow the existing bad system and build a rational society. This will binds us firmly together. We want to fight, we want to fight this current society to the death! However, unfortunately! I had just escaped the shackles of my family, and then I fell into the shackles of my children! In three years, we have had two children in succession! In this way, our so-called efforts and struggles, future careers, and struggles against forces have been largely eliminated by the problems of children and life!

In such a society, there is only one way out: struggle! However, how to struggle? How to solve the problem of children by abandoning them is really difficult to do! Waiting for them to grow up enough and then do other things is even more of a dream! I am suffering every day for this problem, so please give me a guide!

Answer: After reading your letter three times, I can't help but sigh, and the enthusiasm of the lady and her husband to serve society and is overflowing. This is also what the reporter admires endlessly. The lady and her husband are burdened by women and cannot fulfill their ambitions. This is the general situation of young men and women today, and it is by no means trivial as it relates to the future of society. The reporter's anger should be divided into two levels of measures. First level: You two should not have any more children from now on, but ladies, please don't misunderstand. The reporter is by no means an ascetic or a follower of pure extinction. It is to persuade people to cut off the inevitable demands of life. It is to persuade both sexes, in addition to solving the sexual desire problem of two people. Don't create any more side problems 丨childbearing. To solve this problem, I would like to introduce the following two books to the lady: (1) Problems of Birth Control (edited by Cheng Hao, published by Yadong Library); (2) Human Sexual Life (edited by the former person, Yadong Edition). Second level: Since the lady and her husband have already had two children, naturally they cannot abandon them. If there is a wealthy family that is old and childless and happy to accept these two children as adopted children, then you should quickly send them to him, and everyone will be "where they should be." If there is no such adventure, then you have to raise them temporarily. Of course, you can also send them to an orphanage. Besides, there is only one way: the lady should sacrifice herself for the time being and ask the lady's husband to seek a job to make a living, or you two can find a job or other equivalent job. Then put the children in someone else's care or negotiate with the kindergarten specifically and ask them to take care of them. Although it will be a little difficult economically, you two can both free yourselves to work, which will benefit yourselves and society. However, this kind of thing should be handled differently according to each person's environment. What the reporter said is just for reference. And this is not a perfect solution. In short, in today's society, there is no hope of a satisfactory solution to the kind of problem raised by the lady. Speaking of this, it aroused my enthusiasm again; if you two can fight for society and put your own spirit, strength, and love on the suffering masses, then the two children will become secondary or unimportant issues.

Rice Merchants Guild Requests Strict Prohibition of Rice Boat Interception 108

Shanghai City Bean and Rice Merchants Guild, in a petition to the Shanghai Municipal Government, stated: Petition concerning the interception of rice boats, relying on [force to] commit violence; requesting a swift order for police to prohibit [such actions] and severely punish [the perpetrators]. It is alleged that the guild previously received a letter from the Nanbang rice merchants, stating that rice transported from various ports to Shanghai was being forcibly intercepted en route, preventing [the boats] from sailing to Shanghai. A request for a thorough investigation was duly submitted. Now, it is further alleged that a letter was recently received from Shen Shangwen of Yuanyuyu Company, stating that Zhou Xikui, a boat passenger from Pudong, reported that he and Wang Xiangkui, after unloading cargo in Pudong, were sailing empty boats to Nanlu to load goods. On the morning of the day before yesterday, at eleven o'clock, while passing through the Sishi Shoal of Minhang Town, about twenty or thirty people, resembling bandits, claiming to be from the Chuanbang Lianyi Society, chased after them in two boats. They shouted for [the boats] to stop, wielding sharp weapons, jumped onto the boats, assaulted people, destroyed property, and used a large axe to cut down two masts, injuring five boatmen, some seriously and some lightly. During the chaos, many small items were lost. The boats are now docked in Minhang, and [the incident] has been reported to the Jiangsu Water Police of the First District, stationed there, requesting protection and investigation. Meanwhile, [the injured] have gone to the hospital for treatment. It is also heard that those people are still gathering in groups, entrenched in Minhang, deliberately making trouble for boatmen. It is said that the district office has seized a small motorboat, also allegedly belonging to members of the society. Although Zhou Xikui and Wang Xiangkui are not rice merchant passengers, they were still intercepted by members of the Chuanbang Lianyi Society while sailing empty boats from Pudong, and [the society] even dared to injure people and destroy property. Such reliance on [force for] rampant wrongdoing shows a complete disregard for the law. If not urgently admonished and stopped, the situation will escalate, disrupting public order without end. Your esteemed council has always been the leader in rice matters, and even if not for the sake of the rice boats, [you] should consider the livelihood and lives of the people and provide assistance. How can such a disregard for the law and a trend of heinous crimes be ignored and overlooked? Is it because the people of Shanghai will not die from Japanese bullets, but rather be allowed to starve to death? Our guild, in a state of terror, cannot but write this letter to earnestly request upholding justice and providing swift assistance. Given this, it is our opinion that the Lianyi Society, in broad daylight, dares to gather thugs, wield sharp weapons, forcibly intercept rice boats, and injure boatmen. This kind of brutal behavior shows a complete disregard for the law. Moreover, Shanghai is not a rice-producing region, and the entire city's food supply depends on supplies from various ports. If [we] allow gang members to run rampant and intercept boats, the source of rice boats will be cut off, plunging the people of Shanghai into starvation. Regarding public safety, what can be imagined? Therefore, on behalf of the boatmen, we sincerely implore your esteemed council to swiftly submit [this matter] to the Party and government agencies, beseeching them to consider the food supply and lives of the people and boatmen, and to order the military and police to urgently drive out the violent bandits and rescue the intercepted boats, in order to maintain the food supply and secure society. At the same time, it is also reported that two rice-laden boats belonging to Dacheng Company, one detained in Minhang and one in Shagang, etc. Such violence, if not swiftly curbed and severely punished, will deprive rice merchants of their security, and the food supply for the entire city will be immediately affected. Public safety is critically involved, and we are urgently submitting [this report] to the military government, requesting swift and urgent prohibition and strict investigation, in order to punish the violent criminals and protect the good people, so that the law can be upheld and society can maintain order. Approaching the paper, we are filled with urgent anticipation.

Robbery and Disaster Relief Association 109

Two Workers Injured in the Outcome

Fortunately, the Money and Rice Were Retrieved

The Shishan Branch of the Ta Jia disaster relief association in Dachang East City, and the Dachang Office are currently rushing to build workshops and repair roads. There are many workers under its command. The day before yesterday (the 1st) was originally the date for distributing wages. Bandits knew that there would be a large sum of money, so at twelve o'clock at night, they gathered about twenty people and opened the back door of the accounting room, intending to enter and rob it. However, only the young apprentice Zhao Zigao, eighteen years old, and Wang Yougen, twenty-two years old, local residents, were sleeping in the accounting room. After the bandits broke in, they immediately attacked Zhao and others with iron and wooden sticks and bricks, hitting their heads, faces, waists, and backs, causing them to bleed profusely. They immediately fell on the bed, unconscious. Then, they rummaged through chests and boxes, looting recklessly. Unexpectedly, the accountant Zhu [something] had not yet returned from Shanghai to retrieve the money, and there was no large sum of money in the accounting room. As a result, they only robbed Zhu's two trunks, containing one hundred silver dollars, a fur robe, a coat, and many other clothes, as well as twelve cotton quilts belonging to the staff, worth about six hundred dollars in total. After the bandits robbed [these items], they fled. When the two workers woke up and shouted for help, the town's public security bureau and security team were notified and rushed to the scene, but the bandits had already disappeared. The two injured apprentices were sent to the town's [something] Hospital for treatment. However, their injuries were severe, and it is unknown whether their lives can be saved.

Kidnapping Ring Leader Fang Yunlong Captured 111

Female Bandit Also Arrested Simultaneously

Fang Yunlong, a native of Shaoxing, is a well-known kidnapping ring leader in Shaoxing. He has repeatedly committed kidnapping and extortion in Shaoxing and Shanghai. The Shaoxing Public Security Bureau has repeatedly issued arrest warrants, but has been unable to capture him. Recently, Fang suddenly came to Shanghai from Shaoxing. The Shaoxing authorities requested Lu Liankui, the chief Chinese detective of the Shanghai Municipal Police of the Public Concession, to assist in the investigation and arrest. Detective Lu constantly instructed his subordinates to pay close attention to the search and arrest. Until yesterday, detectives Liu Shaokui, Feng Zhiming, and Shao Jingfan learned of Fang's whereabouts and rushed to No. 79 Wuding Road, where they arrested Fang. Then, at No. 8 Changshao Road, they arrested Wang Juhua, a female accomplice and native of Shaoxing. It was learned that Fang and his accomplices had recently kidnapped a young hostage in Hangzhou, and all expenses were provided by Wang. They then searched for the location where the hostage was being held, but Fang's accomplices had already fled upon hearing the news. The two suspects, Fang and Wang, were separately detained. This morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Division of the Special District Court. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that the police had notified the Shaoxing authorities to come to Shanghai to take custody of the suspects, and that further investigation was needed. Therefore, they had not yet formally filed charges, but requested detention in accordance with Article 17 of the Criminal Procedure Law. However, Fang Yunlong had previously committed kidnapping, possession of bombs, and other crimes, and had been repeatedly punished by the court, as evidenced by records. Wang had also been arrested by the police two years ago for kidnapping and transferred to the Zhejiang authorities for interrogation. Last year, she was again discovered by the General Patrol Room for a theft case, but was released by the court due to insufficient evidence. Therefore, the conduct of Fang and Wang is well known, and detention should be granted, [for] one week. Detective Liu then submitted a report detailing the circumstances of the arrest. Qian Hongye, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division, reviewed the report and briefly questioned Fang and Wang, granting approval for detention for one week for further interrogation.

Female Corpse Discovered While Fishing 112

A Shocking Corpse Inside a Large Sack

In a large pond in Dongwangjiazhai, Ningguo Road, Huangxing Road, Yangshupu, Pudong, due to recent rains, the water has accumulated greatly, and there are also fish and shrimp. Shandong people often go there to cast nets and fish. However, the day before yesterday afternoon, they caught a large hemp sack, suspecting it contained valuables. Upon opening it, they found a female corpse inside. The corpse was about twenty-seven or twenty-eight years old, wearing a silk shirt and velvet pants. However, a pair of stone [something] was still tied to the sack. It was determined that the female corpse had been strangled to death and placed in the sack, tied with heavy stones, intending to submerge it in the pond to decompose naturally. After the fishermen discovered it, they were greatly shocked and reported it to the Fourth Precinct of the Fifth District, which immediately investigated the case and searched for the murderer. Yesterday, they ordered the local guarantor Zhou Xiaodi to report it to the local court for autopsy. The court has already appointed Prosecutor Yang and others to the scene to conduct the autopsy, confirming that she was murdered. It was ordered that photographs be taken and the body collected by [something], pending the arrest and investigation of the murderer.

Zheng Chunming Steals Funds from French Consulate 113

Dismissed from His Mother's Job

Stole Large Sums and Was Eventually Arrested

On the 28th of last month, a theft occurred in the residence of Deputy Consul Li Fu (transliteration) on the upper floor of the French Consulate in Nanjing. A total of 1,060 yuan was lost (purely banknotes of five yuan each from the Bank of China). Deputy Consul Li discovered that it was stolen by Zheng Chunming, a servant of his, who had fled to Shanghai with the stolen goods on the Ruhe Steamboat of the Chahe Company. He immediately telegraphed the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, requesting them to pay attention to the pursuit and arrest, and describing Zheng's appearance: about twenty years old, wearing a black wool coat, a leather hat, and a scar on his forehead. Hong, the section chief of the Bureau's Second Section, immediately notified the Water Patrol Team to conduct a strict search and arrest. Li, the deputy captain of the team, led detectives and Cheng Xiqing and Zhang Kefeng, the police chief, to the Yihe Wharf in Hongkou at about 5:00 PM the day before yesterday. Seeing that the Ruhe Steamboat had arrived, they immediately boarded the ship. However, Zheng had already landed and checked into a hotel. They then tracked him down to the hotel. According to the hotel staff, a person matching that description had indeed checked into Room 18, but had gone out for a stroll and would return shortly. They waited there. At about 9:00 PM, Zheng arrived. They immediately rushed forward and arrested him. Knowing that he had been discovered, Zheng had no choice but to surrender. They found 60 yuan in stolen money on his person. After searching his room, they found another 175 yuan in stolen money in a pillow inside his bedding. A total of 235 yuan in banknotes was recovered. The whereabouts of the remaining missing amount is unknown. They took the suspect and the stolen goods to the team. During the preliminary interrogation by Chief Zhu, Zheng Chunming confessed that he was 29 years old and worked as a servant in the French Consulate in the capital. He initially worked in the office, but last year Deputy Consul Li transferred him to the upper floor to perform miscellaneous tasks in his residence. His mother, Hai, 55 years old, worked as a nanny in the home of French Consul Borongde (transliteration). His wife, Zhao, 18 years old, lived with him at No. 18 Hehui Street, Sanpailou, Nanjing. Recently, Consul Bo dismissed his mother due to her old age. His mother was angry and fell ill in bed. He was unable to serve her morning and evening due to his job, which he deeply regretted. He also thought that Deputy Consul Li was temperamental and often scolded him for no reason. He recently heard that Deputy Consul Li was about to return to his country, and his position might not last long. If he could obtain a large sum of money, he could enjoy a comfortable life forever. Therefore, at about 3:00 AM on the 28th of last month, taking advantage of his master's unpreparedness, he secretly stole a large stack of banknotes from the desk in his residence. Due to panic, he did not count the amount at the time, but hid it in the pillow and rolled it into the bedding, leaving only 100 dollars for travel expenses. He then took the bedding and a hand-held rattan basket, sneaked out of the consulate, rushed to the riverbank, bought a ticket from the China Travel Service, and boarded the Ruhe Steamboat to Shanghai. He planned to stay for a few days and then notify his family to return to their hometown to avoid being employed again. When the steamboat arrived, he landed and went to the hotel to rest briefly. He went out to buy a set of sanitary shirts and pants, a wool hat, and a pair of shoes, and took them to the bathroom to wash and dress. He then returned to the hotel with his old leather hat and other items. He went out again, went to a restaurant for a meal, and then went to the Great World for a tour. Upon returning to the hotel, he was arrested. He prepared a document and submitted it to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for verification and approval at about 1:00 PM yesterday.

In the Midst of Fierce Fighting in Rehe, the Anti-Japanese Salvation Movement is Enthusiastic in the Education Sector 115

Representative Mou Mo of the Pingjin Education Association

Reported at the City Principals Conference Yesterday

The Shanghai Education Bureau convened a conference of all school principals in the city at its auditorium at 10:00 AM yesterday. Director Pan of the Education Bureau and over 300 principals from various schools attended. First, Director Pan introduced Mou Mo, a representative of the Pingjin National Institutions of Higher Learning Faculty and Staff Association. Then, Mr. Mou reported on the situation, in addition to the situation of the frontline inspection, and the items needed at the front, which has been reported in various newspapers. The following is a record of the anti-Japanese salvation situation in the Pingjin education sector:

A Glimpse of the Work of the Education Association The Pingjin National Institutions of Higher Learning Faculty and Staff Association has been established for many years and has a very sound organization. Each year, the association fees exceed 1,000 yuan. After the loss of Yuguan, the Pingjin education sector, aware of the panic among the people of Pingjin and the dispersal of students from various schools, urgently sought ways to provide relief. Seven representatives were sent to the front line to distribute 600 yuan worth of comfort items and inspect the actual situation. After the inspection, they deeply understood that the anti-Japanese spirit of our army was reliable, but the material needs were quite urgent. They returned to Ping and promoted [this information] to the public to jointly find ways to provide relief. The Education Association itself deducted 20% of each person's salary, totaling 72,000 yuan, which was remitted to the front line. It also obtained 36 trucks. The Pingda Institute of Technology manufactured 20,000 steel [something] and 30,000 sets of gas masks, all of which have been distributed to various armies.

Elementary School Students Voluntarily Donate Money The most noteworthy aspect of the anti-Japanese work in the Pingjin education sector is the voluntary donation of money by elementary school students. After the Education Association's inspection representatives returned to Ping and reported, the students of various elementary schools convened the Beijing Elementary School Students Federation and decided to request the school authorities of each school to set up a savings box, in which the students of each elementary school would save their spare fruit and money daily and deposit it in the savings box. After it was full, it would be remitted to the anti-Japanese army. As soon as this proposal was made, the schools rushed to prepare [savings boxes]. Each school's savings box was filled in less than two weeks, mostly with copper coins, followed by silver coins. Although the amount was small, it came from the patriotic enthusiasm of the elementary school students and was commendable.

Various Schools Return to Their Original State After the loss of Yuguan, the various schools in Pingjin fell into a state of great chaos, and students dropped out of school. Recently, after the Education Association's inspection representatives returned to Ping, they have returned to their original state and strictly stipulated a rule that any student who does not register within one month of the start of the school term will be expelled. Therefore, in addition to a small number of students who withdrew from school, three-quarters of the students enrolled at the beginning of the current semester have already registered.

Organize the National Education Association Our education sector personnel are intellectual [something] and should be stable, attend classes as usual, and lead the people of all circles to unite in resisting Japan and saving the country. The mission of these representatives in going to the various provinces is to report on the situation of the line, and the biggest request is to contact the education circles in various places and organize a national education association. The most suitable location for this is Shanghai, and a branch will be established in each place. This association will devote all its efforts to leading all sectors in resisting Japan and saving the country during the national crisis, and will study academics in peacetime to develop China's education profession.

Flavored Dragon Beetles and Others 122

On North Szechuan Road, one can see a kind of black, hard-shelled insect sold in Cantonese stores, placed in glass bottles alongside items like "duck gizzards and livers." They are called "Flavored Dragon Beetles." (The name itself is quite flavorful!) Let me tell you, they are delicious! They are sold at Wing On Company's confectionery department for sixty cents a pound. Cantonese people call cockroaches (i.e., oil bugs) [ka zha]. It is said that these dragon beetles are "water ka zha." I haven't been able to find out their scientific name; please advise. In any case, they are six-legged beetles that live in rice paddies, with hairy legs like duck webs. They are caught in the summer, seasoned with "flavored" ingredients, stir-fried until dry, and called flavored dragon beetles. When eating, the legs and shells are removed, and they taste fragrant and salty like peanuts, but with a slight "ka zha" musty flavor. To think that people eat things like this, the Cantonese are truly unbelievable.

A year ago, there was a Japanese performer at the Great World who specialized in eating poisonous insects, especially toads, centipedes, and spiders, causing onlookers to gasp in amazement. I think this is nothing strange. Japanese people are born with monkey-like stomachs that can be filled with anything. A wandering monk can travel all over the island nation eating grass roots and mustard seeds with a small bundle on his back. Compared to them, the Cantonese are just a little more "civilized." Cantonese people eat snakes, rats, turtles, and crabs, with the most poisonous being the most superior. There is also "He Worm." These are basically the same as dung maggots. They are about the size of yellow bean sprouts, colorful, and live in rice paddies. A bowl full of them wriggles and moves. When chopped with a cleaver, the cutting board is full of pulp. When cooked, they resemble crab roe. Otherwise, they can be fried in their original form. If you ask the hundreds of thousands of Cantonese people in Shanghai whether they prefer crab roe or He Worm, they will say, "Ah! There's simply no comparison." But in reality, in Shanghai, they can only eat some "sun-dried He Worm."

Sports 123

To be Held from April 27th to 29th

City-Wide Joint Middle School Sports Meet

Track and Field Divided into Men's and Women's Groups A and B, and Group Performances of Mass Calisthenics

Municipal and Private Approved Middle Schools Must Participate in Track and Field and Mass Calisthenics

| Other Public Middle Schools in the City May Also Participate |

| Participation Method for Secondary Sports Schools Will Be Determined Separately |

The Sports Group of the Health Education Committee of the Municipal Education Bureau held a meeting and resolved to hold the Second City-Wide Joint Middle School Sports Meet this semester. It has been reported in various newspapers. It is understood that the regulations for the sports meet have been approved by the Bureau Affairs Meeting and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and filing. The opening date has been decided for three days, from April 27th to 29th. The sports meet is divided into two parts: group events and track and field. Group calisthenics are divided into mass calisthenics (each school should participate with one-tenth of its students as representatives) and group performances (such as Chinese martial arts, walking exercises, flexibility exercises, game equipment exercises, fitness dances, etc.). Track and field events are divided into men's and women's categories. Men's field events are limited to high jump, long jump, pole vault, discus throw,

Javelin throw, shot put, etc. Six types. Track events are limited to 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 110-meter hurdles, relay

Eight types of 800-meter relay race, 1600-meter relay race, etc. Women's field events are limited to high jump, long jump, javelin throw, shot put, etc. Four types. Track events are limited to 50 meters, 100 meters, 200 meters, 4x100-meter relay race, etc. Four types. Both men's and women's groups are divided into Group A and Group B. All municipal and

And private middle schools that have been approved for establishment must have students participating in track and field and mass calisthenics. However, the participation method for students from secondary sports schools will be determined separately. Other public middle schools in the city are also currently sending students to apply to participate.

The number of winners is based on 15% of the participating athletes as the standard (15 people are selected for 100 participants, 30 people are selected for 200 participants, and so on). During the competition, athletes should proceed according to the designated route. If they run the wrong route, they should return to the original wrong spot and run again. They must not run on the sidewalk, ask for help, obstruct other athletes, or request a guide to lead them.
