Spring and Autumn

The Otter's Puppet State 125

— Zhanlu

A certain surname in Suzhou repaired the stone revetment behind his house. Before the craftsmen had dismantled even half of it, they suddenly discovered a small round pond with a diameter of about two feet. It contained several small fish, swimming freely and happily. A gentle breeze blew across the water, actually creating ripples. Where did the fish come from? Where did the water come from? This aroused the surprise of many workers and onlookers.

If the fish came from the river, this small round pond was five or six feet above the river surface. The fish didn't have wings, so how could they have flown here? As for the source of the water, it was even more incredible. This was accumulated water. It hadn't rained for half a month. Where did the water come from to accumulate in the small pond? Just as they were all guessing, an old farmer happened to pass by and said with a smile, "This is a common thing in the countryside. Digging up a small

fish pond means you can definitely dig up an otter den. Probably this revetment has been around for many years, and there is already an otter den inside. Near the otter den, it must have dug a small pond, drawing clean water from the pond and spitting it into the pond. It also brings small fish into the pond, raising them all year round. When the otter wants to eat fish but is too lazy to go into the water to catch them, it provides the small fish it raises nearby for its food. So, knowing that there is a small fish pond nearby, there must be an otter den." Everyone listened with a mixture of doubt and belief. After continuing to dismantle, they indeed discovered a nest. Although they didn't see an otter, they saw otter fur left in the nest, which confirmed the old farmer's experience.

A pond is originally the kingdom of fish, but this small round pond with a diameter of two feet, arranged by the otter, can only be said to be a pseudo-state organized by the otter | a puppet state. Why does the otter organize this puppet state? It turns out it's to provide food for the otter itself. It's pitiful that these several small fish, about to die, are still happily swimming inside, forgetting that the otter is nearby. Sooner or later, they will become the otter's snack! Comparing the small to the large, this is called the Eastern Otter's Manchurian Fish.

Reflections on Iron Birds from Kites 126

— Rongyu

| So Different from This Day Last Year |

In this time of delightful spring and gentle breezes, as long as you go to play in the countryside, you will always find many lively children flying kites on the open fields covered with green grass. Holding one end of the string, swaying with the wind, the kite, heavier than air, slowly rises. Its situation in the air, I can quote two ancient sentences to describe it, which is what Su Dongpo said: "Vast and boundless, as if riding the wind in emptiness, not knowing where it will stop; drifting and fluttering, as if detached from the world and independent, ascending to immortality." It is truly a worthwhile toy to appreciate!

Thinking back to this day last year. In the sky above Shanghai, no matter whether it was in South Shanghai, Zhabei, the suburbs, or the four villages, where could you see the shadow of kites? Our airspace was filled with the iron birds of the Rising Sun. As long as you heard the grinding sound; and the hovering in twos and threes, the god of terror, the god of destruction, the god of death, these many gods were about to descend! In principle, they come with birds, we go with birds, and we can also show our skills in the air. It's a pity that our iron birds, presumably because their feathers were not fully grown, hid without a trace like kites.

Now, this year, a corner of Shanghai is temporarily at peace. The kites played by children are displaying their style in the sky like stars spread across the sky. However, I hope that next time something happens, our pure white iron birds will be as many as kites. Don't hide in the nest again and be killed like a tiger.

Thinking of iron birds from kites really makes people both cry and laugh. Finally, I also have some small feelings about the evolution of kites.

Some people say that the creation of kites was invented by Han Xin to scout Chu soldiers. There is no record in the official history, I think it is the words of unofficial historians! There is also a record in Du Yi Zhi saying, "Hou Jing besieged Taicheng, and Jianwen released kites to outside the city to ask for reinforcements."

Reading the above legend, it is already known that kites also have the reconnaissance function of iron birds, but in the past they were simpler! Kites have been invented for thousands of years, and they are still like this. The great powers are desperately building iron birds, we must not look at the kites being played and mistakenly think they are our own iron birds!

The Authority of the Residual Flames 127

— Zhang Zhihen

| Destroyed Xiao Xin'an |

Ms. Xiao Xin'an of Yixing burned herself to death in Nanyang. "Her whole body was burning and turned into a fire stick." "The flesh was already charred and could not be saved." How tragic!

Did Ms. Xiao burn to death in the raging, visible flames? I say: "No"; what destroyed Ms. Xiao was the invisible and odorless residual flames of the so-called "old theories" and "old concepts."

"When Ms. Xiao came to Nanyang, her brother strongly opposed it. When the incident was discovered on the ship, her brother was even more regretful and wrote a letter to sever relations with her. Some say this was one of the reasons for the lady's suicide," said the Guowen News Agency:

The general concept of our noble country's society is "keeping to one's place" and "guarding one's own." Even in terms of career issues, it does not advocate "risk" and "creation."

Originally, this kind of concept has a long history and is deeply rooted. Guanzi said: "The son of a scholar will always be a scholar, the son of a farmer will always be a farmer, and the son of a craftsman will always be a craftsman." Han Feizi said: "A family with a constant business will not starve even if they are hungry." From this "constant" and "fixed" career concept, it evolved into the later "keeping to one's place" and "guarding one's own" career concept. Yao Shifu said: "Those who are sons and grandsons must have the ambition to start a business before they can maintain it; they must have the heart to guard against misfortune before they can live in peace." Ji Dakui said: "In all kinds of arts and crafts and doing business, you must always be righteous, abide by the principles of heaven, and be content with your duty. All kinds of risky and empty businesses must not be done." This concept of "maintaining the status quo," "guarding against misfortune," "abiding by the principles of heaven," and "being content with one's duty" has swallowed up countless young people with "adventurous ideas" and a "creative spirit" in China for thousands of years. Although it is said that this man-eating old concept has been reformed a lot recently; however, its residual flames are still burning continuously. The so-called "men" are intimidated by the authority of the residual flames of old concepts and dare not do anything. I don't know how many there are.

The bold Ms. Xiao, as a "woman," actually did not have a "heart to guard against misfortune," did not "keep to her place," crossed the ocean, went to a foreign land, "took the risk" to go to Nanyang, and sought food in other countries. No wonder her brother wanted to "strongly oppose it." Unfortunately, she encountered an unexpected "disaster" on the way. No wonder her brother was "even more regretful and severed relations with her."

The authority of the residual flames destroyed Ms. Xiao of Yixing! It destroyed thousands upon thousands of Ms. Xiaos whose names are unknown!

Hoping for Beauty on the Other Side of the Sky 128

— Chen Yinong

That old man Qu Yuan is really unexpected, he also comes to talk about love, but he is too overestimated, he is neither a pretty boy, nor has omnipotent money, how can he move the heartstrings of a girl to talk about love with him? So, he had to temporarily use his king as a beauty to play a farce of homosexuality and unrequited love. But his achievement is still nothing more than [thinking of beauty, wiping tears and waiting for a gift], and in the end, he still has to ask the old man to be a floating corpse in the Miluo River to conform to the principle after being lovelorn. Blame yourself, what else can be said!

Now there is a modern beauty, who is waiting on the east coast of the Pacific Ocean, coincidentally separated from an old Mr. C, who has the same background as old man Qu, by the Silver River, with tender affection. She grew up in a rich family, and her appearance is as beautiful as a water lily, so she caused that old Mr. C to have a thought of good desire, and he could not sleep or eat. But that beauty, although "sometimes moves with slight容", but also "hesitates and does not come", Mr. C is really dizzy and anxious, so he shouted loudly: [Beauty, I really miss you! I really love you! But you are so cruel, I will be burned for you, please come and save my life! "Although this old Mr. C shouted so loudly, but that beauty, still seemed to hear or not, so a group of dwarfies growing up in Miaodong couldn't help but secretly laughed and said: "Everyone come and see the toad wants to eat swan meat!" I looked at this situation and kept worrying about this honest old Mr. C, so I had to warn him like this:

Old C! Don't be so infatuated. If you continue like this without seeking a new life, then you will become a floating corpse in the Pacific Ocean. Quickly wave the sword of wisdom, cut off the threads of love, and seek self-salvation!

Novel Field Lord 129

— Qin Shouou

A moon like half a cartwheel hung in the center of the pure black sky, the night gradually deepened; half of the fifty warriors lying in ambush in the woods waiting to die were conquered by fatigue and fell asleep, and half gradually slackened because the Wako across the river did not move.

The Wako are the most cunning, the most brutal, the most... things. Suddenly, when the sky was about to dawn and the Tianjia Zhuang people were extremely tired, taking advantage of the wind, countless rockets were shot from the willow forest; in an instant, the air was filled with the stench of sulfur fireballs, and torches flew across the river, and the raging flames were active everywhere. The willow forest immediately became a fire forest.

Needless to say, while the current "Tianjia soldiers" were busy avoiding the fire, the Wako crossed the pontoon bridge. "Children! Today's matter is only death!" The Tianzhuang Lord's big knife was flying in the fire, chopping to death more than a dozen leading Wako, while issuing a decisive order. The second, third, and fifth sons, | the entire team, like madmen, fought with Wako, who outnumbered them by thirty or forty times, in the square in front of the village courtyard, breaking their guns, using swords, breaking swords, using fists, bending fists, kicking, , bumping and roaring, | dying.

The aunt led several women, and none of them retreated. They all irrigated the soil with fresh blood. "Rush in!" Jumping over the square decorated with corpses and bloodstains, the Wako swaggered into the old home of the Tianzhuang Lord. The leaders sat in a hall like demons. "Another one died!" A small fight broke out in the kitchen, and the searching Wako reported that another sick Chinese person had been killed. "Now, all that's left alive here is this dog!" He pointed proudly to a mange-ridden stray dog under the steps.

"Woof: : : Woof: : : Woof" The stray dog ​​seemed to be deliberately feigning illness, and immediately opened a pair of red lamp-like eyes, bared its teeth and claws, pounced on the hall, and desperately bit off the head of the largest leader in the middle. Of course, it was also immediately cut into several pieces by the Wako.

The cock crowed loudly in the distance, and the morning sun lowered the golden red curtain, ending this tragic short play. (End)

Small Recipes

In a Small Restaurant 130

— Luding

Eating and drinking, men and women, these are the great desires of people! Of course, the diet of the wealthy is indeed exquisite. Today it's Sichuan cuisine, tomorrow it's Beijing cuisine, or yesterday it was Western cuisine, or the day after tomorrow it will be Fujian cuisine······

But, like a poor wretch like me, today and tomorrow are the same, yesterday and the day after tomorrow are about the same, there is nothing to write about, even if I write about it, I eat dry rice when I have money, and eat pancakes when I have no money, so what is there to write about? There is no need to write about it.

If I said that I am a noble self-proclaimed hermit, if I said that I am a very person who is satisfied with poverty and peace, it seems that I am not, like the lonely king drunk in the peach palace, like the son banquet in the Zhuangyuan Building, I have never done it, but I do not hope.

Oil and heat, sweetness and deliciousness, are indeed what people like, but big wine and big meat are simply going to kill me, so, I say, small restaurants are better.

Actually, I am not saying that small restaurants will have some good things, and how could I not want to go to a big restaurant like Grandma Liu, but when it comes to big restaurants, I can only think of big restaurants, firstly, I don’t have a foreign outfit on my body, and secondly, I don’t have foreign money in my pocket, 丨 and then? God knows, originally, the reason why big restaurants can be established is that they have their own nobility, their own magic, and their own customers, anyway, small restaurants are the same 丨

The egg fried rice and fish porridge in the small restaurant often make my mouth water, and the two-mao-per-person set meal is really not sloppy at all.

A plate of cabbage, a bowl of clear soup, steaming on the table, people will get familiar with it, and after a long time, maybe add a little bit of delicious coriander, but also add a smiling face and a diligent heart from the waiter.

"Pidgin English" and "Esperanto" 131

— Cao Juren

George Bernard Shaw entertained newspaper reporters in Beiping. Someone asked if he had learned Chinese after arriving in China? Shaw said: "No; I don't know a word. But I am very interested in Pidgin English. Most languages ​​are too constrained by grammar; Pidgin English does not have this drawback. I believe this language may become the future Esperanto." The reporter informed him that Chinese actually does not pay attention to grammar. Shaw said: "Then, Chinese may become Esperanto in the future." (See Tianjin Dagong Bao, February 23)

This passage is interestingly speculated by George Bernard Shaw, and a certain reporter is laughably naive. Western scholars study Chinese characters more from the perspective of sound; and Chinese character scholars emphasize form and meaning, with slightly different directions. George Bernard Shaw's interest in Pidgin English is also due to a different direction. However, the old gentleman certainly does not know that someone had said this before him. About six years ago, Wu Zhihui discussed the national pronunciation and Esperanto. He had already deduced from the standpoint of the world language that Pidgin English has the potential to become the world language. The most important conditions for Esperanto are: first, the spelling method must be simple, and second, the grammatical rules must be simple. Pidgin English has the second advantage, such as:

"The steamer has two eye,

No eye how can see

No can see, how can walk"

(Translation) That ship has two eyes, (referring to the two lights in front)

Without eyes, how can you see,

Cannot see, how can you run.

They use the syntax of Chinese to use the spelling letters of English. Boldly transforming English grammar. This kind of boldness is extremely useful for promoting the progress of the English language. However, if Pidgin English and other languages ​​and writing systems are allowed to grow naturally, after a long period of complex changes in various places, they will still be too constrained by grammar, just like the various existing Western languages. The emergence of Esperanto must be a simple and regular rule, due to human rather than natural growth; it can also be concluded that Pidgin English will not become the future Esperanto.

As for the bastard of a certain reporter, it is simply time to hit the palm of his hand. "Grammar" is a description of science, which is added to the existing status quo for induction, and several principles are obtained from induction, and several exceptions are attached to those that do not conform to the principles. Is there any language in the world that does not pay attention to grammar? There are very many Western scholars who have studied this aspect (see Prof. Gabelentz's (German professor) Chinesische Grammatik (Wen Jingwei). A certain reporter should not lose his soul anymore!

Wandering Monk 132

— Mu Shiying

A few days ago, it snowed heavily. Looking out from the window, the street was deserted, without a living soul. The street seemed narrower than usual; it was so quiet, it had become a street from an ancient painting. Under the eaves of the building across the street, even more desolate than the street, sat a wandering monk, wearing a bamboo hat, eyes closed, a thin robe hanging on his gaunt frame, rhythmically knocking on a large wooden fish. The wind howled, blowing flakes of snow onto him; the snow clung to his collar and melted on his body. I watched and shivered for him, but he remained motionless, still knocking on the wooden fish, without even opening his eyes. I saw an empty rickshaw pull past him. The puller hunched his neck, resting the shafts on his armpit, both hands tucked into his sleeves, slowly pacing along, white mist-like vapor puffing from his mouth.

I saw a woman, bundled up like a goose, her hands tucked under her lapels, a soy sauce bottle peeking out, her ears covered by a velvet hat, a red nose sticking out in front, white mist-like vapor puffing from her nostrils, walking past him, close to the eaves. Her knees seemed frozen stiff, her legs straight, straddling, hobbling along. Afterwards, no one else passed by. The snow fell heavier and heavier, and the sky darkened. Around dusk, I saw a man wearing a crooked, tattered melon-cap, a torn burlap coat, his hair hanging straight down to the collar of his coat, barefoot in heelless shoes, hands in his sleeves, a cigarette butt dangling from the corner of his mouth, wandering past, puffing white mist-like vapor.

But the wandering monk remained motionless, sitting there, rhythmically knocking on the wooden fish—that empty, lonely sound!

At dinner, my mother told the servant to give him a large bowl of rice and a bowl of hot soup. After a while, the servant returned empty-handed, saying, "I left it there."

"Did he eat it?"

"No! He just bowed once and said 'Amitabha.'"

After dinner, I ran out to see him. In the darkness, the sound of the wooden fish echoed, the gray robe still spread on the ground. I asked him:

"Master, you must be hungry, why don't you eat some rice?"

"Amitabha, a monk is used to being cold and hungry." He didn't even open his eyes.

"Where is the Master's temple?"

"At Foguang Temple on Mount Wutai in Shanxi."

"How many years has the Master been a monk?"

Suddenly, he opened his eyes. After a moment, he said, "Twenty-three years."

"Master, why did you become a monk halfway through life?"

He was silent for a long while. "It's a long story. Karma! I was originally from Wutai County. Next door to our house lived a girl—so pure, a lotus flower!" He lowered his head.

I understood.

But then he continued with a long explanation: "At that time, I was a playboy, a scoundrel who specialized in stealing the chastity of virgins. I tempted her every day, yes, I tempted her. Before long, on a summer evening, in the wheat field, this white lotus flower bloomed. One day, she knelt before me, she cried, she said she was pregnant, she begged me to marry her. The poor child, she pleaded so pitifully! But I—I was truly inhuman, I stood up, this child, yes, this child, she was stunned there. That night, I didn't feel anything. Three days later, she died. Some say she hanged herself, others say she died of a sudden illness, but I know how she died. She was buried behind our house. For twelve consecutive nights, I couldn't sleep, I saw this karmic debt kneeling before me, crying. One evening, I ran away, ran to Mount Wutai, rhythmically knocking on the wooden fish, repenting. Until five years ago, when I dreamed of her for five consecutive days. I understood, she felt I hadn't suffered enough. So I came down the mountain, enduring the iron-like hardships in the wind and rain . . . " He began knocking on the wooden fish again.

Returning home, I sat clutching my hair. I heard the sound of the wooden fish, in the quiet, cold night, the rhythmic sound, striking my soul, again and again. Nine o'clock, ten o'clock, eleven o'clock, twelve o'clock . . . hour after hour passed, the sound of the wooden fish just heavily struck my soul. Suddenly, I felt cold all over. I knelt on the ground, in the sound of the wooden fish, I put my palms together, I repented.

Weekly Miscellany (Continued) 133

— Zhang Kebiao

All the texts praising the metropolis invariably center on the night and are built on the foundation of artificiality. However, in reality, does the metropolis truly lack a morning? And upon what foundation are these artificial constructions built? First comes the morning, then the night. If one does not go to the vegetable market early in the morning to purchase ingredients, from where does a sumptuous meal come? The sun rises in the east and shines equally on Avenue Joffre, even if Avenue Joffre may ignore it.

But the metropolis is not just one corner, and Shanghai is not only Avenue Joffre. The sunlight on other roads is also not disregarded. Some mornings leap over certain streets and alleys in Shanghai. For example, what are the mornings like in Xiaoshadu, Caojiadu, Huade Road, and Sun Temple? Isn't the sunlight on the faces, backs, and shoulders of the working masses magnificent? Isn't it more dazzling than the lights on the waists of dancing girls and under the bottoms of wine glasses?

Many people praise the metropolis, many people praise the night. I hope more people will come to praise the morning. At least, the morning has urged me to write the Weekly Miscellany. Someone has written "Shanghai Night Talks," and I cannot help but hope that someone will come out to write "Shanghai Morning Talks."

Night

However, I do not despise the night. The night has its own value, and those who are active at night also have more meaningful activities than the pleasures of the metropolis's residents. For example, petty thieves and bandits who butcher pigs are struggling for a living and not wasting their lives. Some literati and writers often like to write after the night is deep and quiet, and astrologers observe celestial phenomena. Undoubtedly, it is necessary to have darkness. Newspaper editors and printing workers are also destined to work only at night.

Therefore, those who are active at night are not necessarily only rats, bats, owls, prostitutes, and pure metropolitan residents. The beauty of lights does not necessarily have to be felt only in dance halls and bars, because there are also lighthouses that shine all night, indicating the progress of ships in rivers and seas. Even the few streetlights on the road have a unique serenity.

The true charm of the night cannot be appreciated on streets like Avenue Joffre and North Sichuan Road, and even less can it be enjoyed under the lights of dance halls and hotels. Those places give you another kind of intoxication, a kind of muddiness, but that is not what the night wants to give you. I say that what the night gives people is a kind of serenity, like the light and shadow of high-rise buildings illuminated by the streetlights on cold streets; it is a kind of leisure, like the ships moored along the wharves in the Shiliupu area bathed in moonlight; it is a kind of rest, like a baby sleeping soundly in its mother's arms; or it is a kind of tension, like a helmsman at sea watching the lighthouse, like newspaper printing workers engaged in their work.

The unique beauty of the night is in the darkness. Astrologers can only glimpse the secrets of the stars in the darkness, but dance halls are filled with artificial lights. How can the flashlights on the wrists of dancing girls compare to the stars in the sky? The unique beauty of the night is in silence. Writers can only excite their pens in the silence of the quiet night, but how can one be comfortable in the noise of the bars filled with human voices?

The fundamental mistake is that the places where metropolitan residents go do not treat the night as night. They are seeking paintings in the night, which is an inversion. Therefore, they can only seek confusion, because only by being confused can they turn night into a painting. When it comes to resisting nature, they have no part in it. To resist nature, one must first recognize nature, which is what they fear the most. They dare not look nature in the eye, not even dare to look at the sun in the morning. How can one hope to talk about resisting nature!

Only those who sink and fall, their fate cannot be changed. But I am not talking about the destruction of the metropolis, because I said that the metropolis has more than one angle, and the metropolis has a new foundation that can be rebuilt.

The Story of the Black Woman Seeking a God (16) 134

— George Bernard Shaw, translated by Yi Xian

"According to this, is there anything to comfort us?" Mr. Croker said. "We are bound to perish anyway." "Not necessarily," said the first gentleman.

"Definitely," Mr. Croker said sternly. "The temperature conditions in which life can exist are already known and beyond question. You cannot live in freezing temperatures, nor can you live in the heat of a furnace. Whichever of these temperatures the Earth reaches, we are bound to perish."

"No!" said the first gentleman. "These temperatures you speak of are only harmful to a part of us, namely our bodies. Our bodies die within a few years, often in those airy bedrooms where the temperature is kept very comfortable. But what about the thing that makes the difference between a living body and a dead body? Is there any evidence, any possibility, that its existence depends to any great extent on temperature? Although it has the strange quality of creating for itself those forms of flesh, it is certainly not blood, nor flesh, nor bone. It is something intangible. If you try to define it, you must think of it as an electromagnetic wave, as a vibration rate, as a spinning of wood, or if the ether exists, in other words, as such a thing. If this thing exists—and who can doubt its existence?—then it can exist on the coldest dead star, or in the hottest fiery mouth of the sun."

"Then," said one of the ladies, "how do you know the sun is hot?"

"What a strange question!" Mr. Croker said scornfully. "I feel it's hot, I know it."

"You feel pepper is hot," said the lady, returning his scorn with flavor. "But you can't light a match with it."

"You feel that the notes on the right end of a piano keyboard are higher than the notes on the left side; but both notes are on the same plane," said another lady.

Not Considering Success or Failure

The Japanese are using the old trick of destroying Korea, supporting Pu as a puppet. In less than two years, they will repeat the performance of the deposed Korean prince. When Tang spoke, there was also a certain foreign military officer present, who was moved. (3rd, Special Dispatch)

After the establishment of the pseudo-state, it declared to the outside world that he was also an official of the pseudo-state. In fact, he has never had any dealings with the pseudo-state. Since September 18th, he has only known to defend the country and protect the people. Japan invades our country, and he can only resist bravely to fulfill his duty as a soldier. Success or failure is not a consideration. This time, the Japanese army attacked Rehe and fabricated public opinion. In fact, our thirty million compatriots in the three northeastern provinces, under the oppression of power, do not want to be double slaves and are eagerly looking forward to the government recovering the lost territory. This is the true intention of the people of the Northeast. Recalling when Japan destroyed Korea, it initially retained the position of the prince, but soon destroyed him. Today, Japan supports Puyi as a puppet ruler in the Northeast. I dare to assert that Puyi's position will be completely destroyed in less than two years. We have a lesson from the past, so at this time when the Japanese invaders are launching a large-scale attack on Rehe, our people and government should jointly rise up to resist the insult. He has a responsibility to defend the territory and will shed his blood and do his best to deal with the Japanese to the end. (3rd, Special Dispatch)

The situation there is now very critical. Tang also said that he wants the world to know that he will fight to the end. Tang looked tired and, after talking with the Reuters correspondent, set off for the front line to supervise the battle. (3rd, Reuters)

(Reuters, London, March 3) In the past few days, the Chinese embassy in London has been surrounded by hundreds of British people who volunteered to participate in the war in Rehe and serve China. Among them are many veterans, as well as some doctors, and there are also people who intend to take stomach risks. There are also many British women who are willing to serve as nurses. It is reported that the Chinese embassy expressed its gratitude to the volunteers, but said that the embassy had no plans to accept their requests.

(Reuters, London, March 2) The Chinese in London are now paying close attention to the news of the war in Rehe reported in newspapers and broadcast on the radio. All are willing to do their best to support the Chinese army at the front. Members of the Chinese Seamen's and Laborers' Association have agreed to donate a portion of their wages every week. Sailors who earn only two pounds a week donate as much as ten shillings a week.

League of Nations 139

Reasons for My Resignation

The Focus of the Sino-Japanese Situation Shifts from Geneva

The Government Should Vigorously Resist the Japanese Army in Jehol

(Geneva) Dr. Wellington Koo, in an interview with Reuters last night, confirmed that he and Representatives Yen and Quo had resigned from their positions as representatives to the League of Nations in Nanjing. However, he stated that after they inquired with the government about its position and plans, they received a reply and agreed to continue serving. Dr. Koo also mentioned that, in the opinion of the representatives in Geneva, the Chinese government should appoint new figures to the League of Nations to express their views, as the current representatives have been working for a long time and are now exhausted. They feel that one act of the Sino-Japanese dispute has now ended, and the focus of the Sino-Japanese situation has shifted from Geneva to Jehol. China should provide a very strong resistance to the Japanese army in Jehol, which is the main reason for their resignation. (Reuters Dispatch, 2nd)

Central Government Sends Telegram to Persuade Them to Stay

Yesterday, a Geneva dispatch reported that the three Chinese representatives to the League of Nations, Yen Hui-ching, Wellington Koo, and Quo Tai-chi, had telegraphed Nanjing, resigning from their positions. A Central News Agency reporter specifically inquired about this matter this morning with a prominent figure who had just arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing. According to him, the three representatives' request to resign had been a fact for several days. The three representatives intended to express that, as of today, the only way to resist Japanese aggression is through desperate resistance. However, the government had already resolved to resist Japan, so the Central Political Council had already decided to send a telegram of reassurance the day before (the 1st), instructing them of the government's determination to resist and adopting all the proposed opinions.

Embargo on Arms

Britain Did Not Invite the United States to Participate

League of Nations Discusses Embargo on South America

(Washington) According to Undersecretary of State Castle today, Britain did not invite the United States to participate in the embargo on arms exports to the Far East, and the U.S. State Department has not received any notes from Britain regarding an arms embargo. (Reuters Dispatch, 2nd)

(London) Sir Hamilton, who was appointed as the President of the University of Edinburgh, gave a speech to the students today, greatly criticizing the British government's method of prohibiting the shipment of arms to the Far East without distinguishing between aggressor and victim. The audience expressed great dissatisfaction with Japan. (Havas Dispatch, 2nd)

(Geneva) The Council of the League of Nations today passed a plan to prohibit the shipment of arms to Paraguay and Bolivia and will invite the United States to participate in this cooperation. The Council will soon reconvene to discuss the actions to be taken regarding the South American dispute. (Reuters Dispatch, 2nd)

(Geneva) Regarding the prohibition of arms shipments to Bolivia and Paraguay, after proposals were made by Britain and France, the Secretariat of the League of Nations seemed prepared to draft a declaration. The representatives of the Council of the League of Nations recently held an informal meeting to discuss how to draft the question. After this declaration is passed by the Council, it will be submitted to countries that manufacture arms, countries that transport arms in transit, and other countries, asking them to sign. The major powers are very cautious about this matter. Therefore, this declaration must first be recognized individually by the representatives of the Council, and after a formal discussion by the Council, it can be distributed to the governments of various countries for their approval. A press release from the Secretariat of the League of Nations stated that, regarding the Anglo-French proposal to prohibit arms shipments to Bolivia and Paraguay, the three-member committee of the League of Nations responsible for inspecting the dispute between the two countries today requested opinions from countries other than Britain and France. The three-member committee has put forward detailed suggestions to allow the countries that agree to participate in this action to consider and coordinate their actions. The suggestions of the three-member committee include three items: (1) How to declare a commitment not to directly or indirectly export and sell arms to the parties involved; (2) Specify what types of arms should be prohibited; (3) Agree on ways to coordinate actions with each other; (4) Stipulate under what conditions each government considers its declaration to be effective and notify each other. The three-member committee declares that it intends to ask the Secretary-General of the League of Nations to include the issue of implementing Article 11 of the Covenant on the Council's agenda. (Havas Dispatch, 2nd)

Snowfall in Peiping

From Last Night Until This Morning

Four to Five Inches of Snow on the Ground

(Peiping) It snowed from 11:00 PM last night until 9:00 AM this morning. The snow accumulated to four or five inches on the ground, the first heavy snowfall since winter began. (Special Dispatch, 3rd)

Earthquake in Japan Early This Morning

Reuters, Tokyo, March 3rd: At 2:30 AM this morning, Tokyo suddenly felt a very strong earthquake, which lasted for quite a while, causing great panic. Although the city only suffered minor damage, 1,500 houses in Kamaishi and Iwate were swept away by a large tidal wave caused by the earthquake. According to investigations, Kamaishi was the hardest hit, and many villages and towns along the northeast coast also suffered the same fate. The houses were either destroyed by the earthquake or swept away by the tidal wave.

Reuters, London, 2nd: The seismograph at the West Bromwich Observatory indicated that there was a large earthquake 6,000 miles away at 5:43 PM today, which lasted until 9:00 PM. The tremor was so strong that the instrument's rod also vibrated out of its socket, making it impossible to obtain complete records. According to the observatory director, Shaw, this was the largest earthquake he had experienced in his 28 years.

Reuters, Tokyo, 3rd: Japan experienced a very strong earthquake early this morning, causing significant loss of life and property in several places. It is now believed that the epicenter of the earthquake was the island of Kinkasan, east of Matsushima. Matsushima is one of Japan's three major scenic spots. In 1896, Kinkasan experienced a tsunami that destroyed the entire northeast coast, killing 30,000 people. Today's tidal wave occurred 40 minutes after the earthquake and was about four to ten feet high. The northeast coast of the main island, 300 miles long, was affected, with the affected area extending from Ishinomaki, east of Matsushima, to Shiriyazaki at the northernmost tip of the island. Even Hokkaido was affected. The area with the most earthquake fatalities was Omoto, with more than 100 deaths. Elsewhere, the number of deaths ranged from a few to dozens. Countless houses were destroyed and fishing boats sunk.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd: At 2:35 AM this morning, a strong earthquake, rarely seen in recent years, occurred in Tokyo, the Kanto region, the Tohoku region, and Hokkaido. According to the Central Meteorological Observatory, the maximum amplitude was 40 millimeters, comparable to the large earthquake in Izu in previous years.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd: The Naval Ministry announced that at 9:00 AM today, the Yokosuka Naval District dispatched two flying boats from Kashiwada and one flying boat from Tateyama to investigate the earthquake disaster. Also, at 7:30 AM, the 1st and 6th Destroyer Squadrons were ordered to dispatch six ships.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd: The major earthquake this morning occurred in the middle of the night, causing great anxiety among the citizens. However, as of now, there has been no major damage in the Kanto region. The most severely affected areas were the Kamihei and Shimohei districts of Iwate Prefecture. In Kamaishi Town, in addition to 1,500 houses being swept away by the tidal wave, a fire broke out, burning down 300 houses. It is still burning and there is no way to extinguish it. In the Miyako area, more than 250 houses were washed away. In addition, the damage is very severe in various parts of the prefecture. Details are unknown due to communication disruptions. Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd: When the earthquake occurred at 2:30 AM this morning, a large wave struck the coast of Iwate Prefecture. In the Kuwazaki area, dozens of houses collapsed, and the coastal area seems to have been completely destroyed. Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd: Due to the strong earthquake this morning, a large wave occurred in the Sanriku area. In Kamaishi Town, 1,500 houses were washed away by the wave, and at the same time, a fire broke out, burning down 300 houses. It is still burning. At 3:00 AM, a fire also broke out in the Tadaoshi Village area. 250 houses were washed away in Miyako Town, and the Yamada area seems to have been completely destroyed.

Nichiren, Morioka, 3rd: At 2:30 AM on the morning of the 3rd, a strong earthquake, unseen in decades, occurred in the Iwate Prefecture area. All kinds of power lines were cut, turning the area into a world of darkness. After a dozen minutes, a violent tsunami occurred along the Pacific coast. According to reports received by the prefectural authorities, the state of damage before 7:00 AM this morning was as follows: 256 houses collapsed in Miyako Town, 1,500 houses were washed away in Kamaishi, and fires broke out in various parts of the city, burning down hundreds of houses and still spreading. Residents have all fled to the mountains with nothing but their clothes. The damage in Otuchi Town is also great, and Funakoshi Village has been completely destroyed.

Nichiren, Morioka, 3rd: In Miyako Town, Iwate Prefecture, a huge wave of more than ten feet swept up the Miyako River, which flows through the center of the city, washing away more than twenty motorized boats. The Miyako Bridge was destroyed, cutting off traffic. The cries of citizens continued throughout the night.

Nichiren, Morioka, 3rd: The current state of earthquake damage in this prefecture, as investigated, is as follows:

(1) Tanohata Village: 182 houses washed away, 12 dead, 45 missing.

(2) Omoto Village: 80 houses washed away, more than 100 dead.

(3) Fudai Village: 87 houses washed away, 1 dead, 2 children missing.

(4) Kesennuma Town: 40 houses washed away.

(5) Yonesaki Village: 4 houses washed away, 7 dead.

(6) Ube Village: 6 houses washed away, 7 missing.

New President Roosevelt

Inauguration Ceremony Simplified

Economic Cleanup Plan

Reuters, Washington, 3rd: Roosevelt appointed Rear Admiral Grayson as the director of the preparatory committee for the new president's inauguration ceremony. Roosevelt advocated for a simplified ceremony but has agreed to a day of celebration. The official ballroom dance, which was abolished by former President Wilson, will be revived. The Democratic Party won a major victory in the general election last November, so the president's inauguration ceremony will have the flavor of a Democratic celebration. Most of the newly elected governors of the 38 Democratic states will come to Washington to participate in the grand ceremony. The person supervising the oath will be Attorney General Hughes. If the weather is fine, the ceremony will be held in the open square outside the Capitol, but if the weather is bad, the ceremony will be held indoors, and only a small portion of the 100,000 spectators will be allowed to enter.

Reuters, Washington, 3rd: Congress will grant the new president the power to reorganize the structure of government departments. Experienced inspectors generally acknowledge that the new president will exercise this power. Roosevelt's close advisors have been preparing economic matters for several weeks, but the contents are kept secret, which shows that Roosevelt intends to conduct a major cleanup. The relief plan under the economic plan grants Roosevelt the power to cut hundreds of millions of dollars in budget expenditures. The relief plan is currently in the final stages of negotiation in Congress. In addition to the ten administrative departments of the cabinet, the new president can abolish or merge any executive agencies in the ten departments to save expenses, but he cannot abolish their functions, because any political affairs decided by Congress must be implemented.

Reuters, Wilson, 3rd: Walsh, who was traveling to Washington to take office as Attorney General, suddenly suffered a heart attack in the car at 7:10 PM tonight and died. His remains have been moved to a funeral home for burial. His wife, who had just been married for a week, was also in the car and is now said to be overwhelmed with grief and mentally distraught. The successor to the position of Attorney General will likely be lawyer Mullen.

Havas, Washington, 2nd: New President Roosevelt departed from New York tonight and will meet with President Hoover tomorrow. It is generally believed that Roosevelt and Hoover will discuss the economic situation. New President Roosevelt has recently appointed former Ambassador to Belgium, Phillips, as Undersecretary of State.

More Than Two Thousand Detained in Two Days

The Election Campaign Is Just a Sham

Reuters, Berlin, 2nd: The cabinet decided to hold the opening ceremony of the new Reichstag in the garrison church of Potsdam. Communists and socialists will probably not be allowed to participate, so it will be easy for the government to announce an indefinite postponement after the opening and then proceed with its four-year plan. It is expected that the Reichstag will be convened on April 4. The current election campaign has become a one-sided affair, and the public pays very little attention to it. However, it is expected that at least 85% of voters will vote on Sunday. The Socialists are confident that they will be able to greatly increase their votes and expect that the National Socialists will definitely not be able to win a complete victory as they hope. The National Socialists are still carrying out a large-scale purge of the Communists. In the past two days, more than two thousand people have been arrested in Rhineland and Westphalia. Stammfer, the editor-in-chief of the Socialist newspaper Vorwärts, was also arrested early this morning because he signed a declaration criticizing the government's closure of Social Democratic Party newspapers as illegal. This statement has been denied by the authorities, who claimed that the police searched for him but did not find him. The cabinet has decided to ban foreign journalists from spreading information that is inconsistent with the German government's news. Prussian Interior Minister Göring broadcast a speech today, stating that the government is determined to eradicate communism, but there is no danger if the Socialists or Communists engage in propaganda within the legal scope.

Shanghai Bank in the Capital is Robbed

Located in a Vital Area

In Broad Daylight

All Circles Are Surprised

(Nanjing) At 10:30 AM on the 3rd, the Shanghai Bank at the intersection of Zhuque Road was robbed. Two robbers, each carrying a pistol, stood guard at the gate. One was wearing a gray camel hair robe and a felt hat, and the other was wearing a blue short coat, looking like a worker, both about twenty years old. One robber entered and jumped into the counter. At that time, cash and foreign currency were being collected. He searched the table and drawers, stealing more than 3,020 yuan in cash and banknotes. Another customer, Zhang Xintai, had just exchanged 950 yuan in silver dollars at the bank and was about to leave when the robber noticed him and robbed him as well. By the time the military police arrived after hearing the news, the robbers had already escaped without a trace. After inquiring with the bank to confirm the details, a team was dispatched to investigate. All circles in the capital were surprised that such a serious robbery occurred in a vital area during broad daylight. At around 12:00 PM, crowds of onlookers were still gathering in front of the bank. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

Song Ziwen Delivers Important Speech 140

Already Telegraphing Luo Wen-gan About the League of Nations Representatives' Resignation

Should Use Utmost Effort to Resist in Jehol

Rumors Circulating Are Familiar Japanese Propaganda Tactics

Decided to Continue Suspending Boxer Indemnity Payments for Another Year

Acting Premier Song Ziwen, accompanied by Secretary Huang Chundao and Zhang Xueliang's Western advisor, Donald, flew from Nanjing to Shanghai yesterday morning to discuss the financial problems of North China with the financial community. At 11:00 AM this morning, Song met with reporters from various newspapers at his residence on Qiqi Road and delivered an important speech. Details are as follows:

Resignation of the Three Representatives

The reporter first asked about the Reuters dispatch this morning that our country's League of Nations representatives, Yan Huiqing, Wellington Koo, and Guo Taiqi, had telegraphed Nanjing to resign.

What is the truth? Song replied that he had not heard anything about it and planned to immediately telegraph Foreign Minister Luo Wengan to inquire about the truth.

Uncertainty About Going North

When asked when he would go north, he said that his trip north was still undecided and would depend on the practical needs in the future. His visit to Shanghai this time was (1) to inspect the minting of new coins at the mint and (2) to discuss various financial matters.

The Battle of Jehol

Regarding the battle of Jehol, telegrams have been frequently reporting in recent days that our army has suffered many setbacks. The reporter asked Song about the truth of the battle of Jehol this morning. Song said that the battle of Jehol initially took place in the railway area, where the Japanese side had various transportation conveniences. Our army had to change its lines for strategic reasons. Now, our army is holding firmly to the dangerous positions and will use our utmost efforts to resist desperately. Success or failure is not a matter of concern. As for rumors of Sun Dianying's surrender and the defection of the volunteer army, these are familiar Japanese propaganda tactics and are not worth refuting.

Abolishing the Tael and Changing to the Yuan

Song also stated that the abolition of the tael and the change to the yuan was originally scheduled to take effect on March 1, but because he had been away from Nanjing for many days and had not made any arrangements, it had to be postponed. The currency system regulations have been submitted to the Central Political Council for discussion and passed yesterday and can be submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review today, which should not be a problem.

20 Million National Treasury Bonds

Song also said that the 20 million national salvation treasury bonds were decided by the Beiping Political Affairs Committee and approved by the Central Political Council. The committee planned to use 500,000 yuan from the cigarette tax allocated to the committee by the central government each month as a fund to issue the bonds in Tianjin and Beiping. There has been much speculation from the outside world, but these are not the facts.

Boxer Indemnity Suspended for One Year

Song also stated that the Boxer Indemnity from various countries has been decided to be suspended for another year. However, the U.S. portion will be allocated to Tsinghua School expenses and the China Cultural and Educational Association Fund, as in the previous year. Although the Boxer Indemnity is suspended, the allocations will continue. As for the Japanese merchants refusing to pay Chinese customs duties at the checkpoints, we have lodged a strong protest and are negotiating with them.

Japanese Warships Spy on Our Coast

The Outer Sea Police Department received a report that a Japanese warship was found in the waters off Shengshan Island. It first sailed on the sea and then went to the coastal ports to spy, intending to inspect the defenses of our coast. Several fishing boats there were planning to follow the Japanese warship to observe its movements, but they could not catch up because the Japanese warship was very fast. The Outer Sea Department has already sent telegrams to the First and Third Teams of Shenjiamen and Dinghai to quickly dispatch patrol boats to investigate the warship's movements, and at the same time, it has ordered coastal areas to be on alert.

Ministry of Finance Instructs Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to Calculate Transactions Using Silver Coins 141

Must Not Use Silver Taels After March 10th

The Ministry of Finance instructed the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, saying: To ensure compliance, the Ministry, in preparation for abolishing the tael, stipulates that the common silver taels in Shanghai and the silver standard coin of one yuan, or the old one-yuan silver coin with its original weight and fineness, should be converted at a fixed exchange rate of 7 qian 1 fen 5 li per yuan. This will take effect on March 10th of this year, as announced by the Ministry, and will be distributed to the Shanghai Silver and Money Industry Associations for compliance. All stores in Shanghai, regardless of their business, must, from that date, uniformly calculate the prices of goods and all transactions in silver coins and must no longer use silver taels in order to emphasize the law and unify the system. You are hereby instructed to forward this order to all trade associations for their compliance. This order.

This newspaper has obtained a special list of exchange rate calculation methods, as follows: One silver standard coin = 23.493448 grams of pure silver.

Every tael of Shanghai silver contains 33.599 grams of pure silver.

Liang Shiyi Arrives in Shanghai This Morning 142

Gongchuo, Qian Xinzhi, and Others Go to the Wharf to Welcome Him

To Go North in Ten Days to Participate in the War of Resistance

Before Departure, He Will Visit His Old Friend Duan Qirui for a Chat

Liang Shiyi, the former Minister of Finance of the Beijing Government, arrived in Shanghai this morning at 8:30 a.m. aboard the President Coolidge of the Dollar Steamship Company from Hong Kong. He landed at the Xinkang Wharf. According to Liang's statement to a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, he will stay in Shanghai for more than twenty days before going north to participate in the War of Resistance. A second world war may be possible, but it will definitely not be for our country. The Chinese people's reliance on others is no different from a policy of suicide. In the future, the whole country should unite and fight to the end to win the final victory. The news of Liang's arrival in Shanghai is recorded below:

Arrival Situation

The President Coolidge entered the port at 4:25 a.m. and berthed at Floating Pontoon No. 16 in Yangshupu at 6:00 a.m. Liang transferred to a small boat at 8:30 a.m. and landed at the Xinkang Wharf. With him were Cen Xuepin and three others. More than forty of Liang's relatives and friends, including Ye Gongchuo, Qian Xinzhi, Zheng Baozhao, and Sa Tongsheng, went to the wharf to welcome him. Liang was wearing a purple-brown satin robe and a black satin mandarin jacket. His beard and eyebrows were mottled with white, and he was already sixty-five years old. However, he was in high spirits and showed no signs of senility.

Participating in the War of Resistance

Liang said that he would stay in Shanghai for more than twenty days and then go north to Ping to participate in the work of resisting Japan and saving the country. This work is the natural duty of all people in the country. Even a three-year-old child should participate in this work. When I leave Shanghai to go north, I do not intend to enter Beijing to become an official, but participating in political work is another matter. All citizens should understand and be concerned about the country's politics.

World War

Liang continued, "We have no way of interfering in the international situation. If we want to intervene, we must first consider our capabilities. Otherwise, how can we ask? A second world war may occur, but this war will definitely not be caused by our country or the Sino-Japanese issue. It's like two people fighting in the road, and a third party joins in, with different purposes. The Chinese people's reliance on others is no different from a policy of suicide. To survive, we must all fight to the end to win the final victory."

Japan as a Mad Dog

Liang said that Japan's various barbaric and unreasonable acts of aggression are like a mad dog. There is no need to criticize them, and there is no room for negotiation. If they invade, we can only resist.

Will Meet Duan

Liang also said that Liang and Duan Qirui are old friends, so he will visit him after arriving in Shanghai, but the date has not been determined. I rarely go out or speak while living in Hong Kong, except for reading. I have not met Hu Hanmin, but I met Tang Shaoyi once a few years ago. As for the commercial situation in Guangdong, it is more deserted than before, probably due to the impact of the world economy. Finally, the reporter asked if he was invited to go north by Zhang Hanqing by telegram. He strongly denied it, saying that there was no such thing.

Xie Moude Wields a Sharp Blade

Chops at His Companions in the Middle of the Night

Hasn't Slept All Night, Continuously Chopping at Several Friends

Sharp Kitchen Knife Soaked in Blood

Xie Moude, a trainee at the Oriental Trust Company at 323 Fujian Road, is a 19-year-old from Nanjing. He has been working at the company for two years. He usually behaves in a well-behaved manner and gets along well with his colleagues. In the past two years, he has never had any ill feelings with anyone, and he has no suspicion or gap with Wang Ruixu, Gu Xuetong, Xia Fengfei, etc., who live in the same room. Last night, Wang Ruixu and his colleague Wang Wencheng, who lived in the neighboring room, went out to the theater to watch a play. When they returned at midnight, they still talked with Xie for a while before going to bed. Everyone was dreaming, but Xie got out of bed alone, wearing only a short shirt and a pair of military pants, barefoot and wearing shoes, holding a brand-new sharp kitchen knife in his hand, and chopped at the heads and faces of Gu Xuetong, Xia Fengfei, and Wang Ruixu, who were lying in the same room, in order. Gu's lips and Xia's head were cut. The two woke up in pain from their dreams, but they did not suspect that Xie was using a knife to treat them. They only thought that they were fighting because of nightmares, so they endured the pain and did not argue with him. However, Xie still scolded and continued to chop at Wang Ruixu, who was lying on the bed. Fortunately, Wang was sleeping with his head covered by the quilt. Although he was chopped several times, he was protected by the cotton quilt and was unscathed. Unexpectedly, Xie still did not stop after chopping everyone in the same room. He broke into the front room and chopped at Wang Wencheng's head and face, who was sleeping soundly. At this time, the clock struck two. The injured people got up one after another, and Xie fled out of the room and tightly pulled the door with his hand, so that everyone could not open the door to chase him. He then abandoned the knife and fled. As soon as he left the company's gate, the doorman and patrol of the company saw his condition and heard the noise in the room. Suspecting him, they questioned him. He claimed that his colleagues in the room were joking and there was nothing else. After deceiving the patrol, he ran to the room opened by Jiang Fachang, the captain of the detective team of the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau, at 314 Dachunghua Hotel on Xizang Road to hide. Jiang and Xie were friends. Jiang came to Shanghai this time and stayed at the hotel, and he had invited Xie to meet. Therefore, Xie hurriedly escaped to that place after the accident. As for the injured people, after Xie left the room, they discovered under the light that everyone's heads and faces were bleeding. Gu Xuetong's upper lip had also been cut off. Everyone was shocked and realized that Xie was not a nightmare and actually wanted to murder them. They advocated reporting to the authorities for investigation. Therefore, the doorman and patrol reported to the Old Gate Patrol Station and dispatched detective Feng Xiushan to the company to investigate. They found the murder weapon and sent the three injured people to the hospital. Gu was the most seriously injured and was hospitalized for treatment. Wang and Xia were slightly injured and were discharged from the hospital that night after applying medicine. Then, Detective Feng inquired about Xie Moude's usual whereabouts and went to Dachunghua Hotel to arrest him. He was arrested in Jiang's inner room. Jiang was also implicated. After the head of the patrol questioned him in detail, he ordered Jiang to be a witness, and Xie was detained. This morning, he was escorted to the First Special District Court. Judge Feng Shide interrogated him. All the victims except Gu arrived in court. They all said that they had no grudges against Xie and that Xie was usually very kind to others. Xie confessed that he slept well last night and did not know why he did this. The court then asked about the origin of the murder weapon. Xie said that he met a prostitute named Xueying at the game hall and fell in love with her. Last Friday and Saturday, he went to Room 304 of the Xinhuizhong Hostel with the prostitute. After spending the night together, the prostitute decided to form a family with him and asked him to buy all the furniture, so he first bought this knife, etc. The patrol lawyer, Dang Baoyi, said that Xie's murder weapon was prepared in advance, and he had no mental illness, so it was difficult to escape the crime under Article 284, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. However, the case still needs to be investigated, so he requested an extension. Judge Feng then ordered the defendant to be returned to custody and rescheduled the hearing for seven days.

Vietnamese Police Murder Case

The Chamber of Commerce Presents a Serious Representation to the Municipal Government

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a serious representation to the Municipal Government regarding the Vietnamese police murder case. The original text roughly stated: "According to a letter from the Chaozhou Association in Shanghai, our association received a letter from our fellow villager Zhu Guhan, stating that his younger brother, Zhu Guting, a native of Chaoyang, 20 years old, was a shop assistant at Renhe Store on Xinqiao Street in the French Concession. At 1:30 p.m. on the 25th of this month, he was passing by the Ningbo Hotel on Xinqiao Street in the French Concession when the Vietnamese police opened fire to disperse the crowd. Zhu Guting failed to escape and was shot in the chest, killing him on the spot. His elderly parents and young wife and children were left behind. How can they live after this tragedy? We implore you to help us redress the injustice." The letter stated that the Vietnamese police arbitrarily opened fire to disperse the crowd, injuring and killing passersby, which was an abuse of power, a violation of the law, and intentional homicide. If they are not severely punished, the citizens will be in danger at all times. In addition to sending a telegram to the Municipal Government to make a serious representation to the French Concession authorities, to punish the murderers according to the law, to provide generous compensation to the family of the deceased, and to guarantee that such incidents will not happen again in the future, to respect human life and provide protection, we should also send a telegram to uphold justice and provide assistance. The case of the Vietnamese police injuring people in the French Concession happened once before, but it was vaguely closed at the time, which led to recklessness. Today, a Chinese person was shot to death due to a minor police matter, and two people were shot and injured. If this case cannot be punished according to the law, the lives of the residents of the French Concession will be in a state of insecurity. It is reasonable to submit this to Your Excellency for review and urge you to make a serious representation to the French Consul so as to achieve the purpose of punishing the murderers and compensating the victims. This is for the public good. Respectfully submitted to the Municipal Government."

Three Child Laborers Lured by Communists to Become Red Army Soldiers

Zhu Changyou, a child from Anhui, is 17 years old and lives at 34 Huade Road. Xue Zhengtao, a child from Shandong, is 15 years old and lives at 311 Taopeng Road. Fan Xiaoerzi, a child from Qingjiang, is 18 years old and lives in a bungalow without a number on Longjiang Road. The three children were child laborers at the British American Tobacco Company at 17 Huade Road. Suddenly, at about 5:00 p.m. on the 27th of last month, after receiving their wages from the company, they disappeared at the same time. Their families, Zhu Xinhe, Xue Zheng, Fan Yongfu, etc., searched everywhere, but there was no news. Later, Zhai Chunhua and Jiang Chunfang, colleagues of the tobacco company, learned that the three children had been deceived by the communists to join the Red Army. They notified Zhu Xinhe, who then reported to the Yulin Road Patrol Station with Xue and Fan based on the information. Detective Xie Wanfang and a Western detective arrested Wang Daren, a 20-year-old from Qingkou, at the corner of Kunming Road. He confessed that his accomplice was Wang Jinde, a 24-year-old from Guangdong, who lived in a pavilion at 139 Jiaxing Road. They secretly went to the address and arrested him, seizing a large number of reactionary books, and took them to the patrol station for detention. This morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Division of the Second High Branch Court. Patrol lawyer Gan Jingxian stated the previous situation and requested an extension, saying that the two defendants admitted that they had joined the Communist Party in the patrol station. He presented various reactionary books for inspection. Then, Zhu Xinhe, Xue Zheng, Fan Yongfu, and witnesses Zhai Chunhua and Jiang Chunfang testified about the process. Zhai and Jiang claimed that the first defendant, Wang Daren, often came to the company gate at noon when the child laborers were released for lunch and talked and played with the three missing children, giving them pencils and notebooks, and telling them to go to Hankou to become Red Army soldiers. Judge Qing Zhao questioned the two defendants and ordered them to be returned to custody and rescheduled the hearing to investigate and cross-examine them.

National Coal Relief Association

Requests Exemption from Coal Subsidy Fee

In addition to paying the mining area and production and sales tax every year, the coal sold in Shandong Province must also pay a temporary subsidy fee of 30 cents per ton. In July of last year, the National Coal Relief Committee of this port, considering that foreign coal was dumped and domestic coal was difficult to survive, submitted a request to the authorities for exemption. The exemption was granted for three months. Now that the exemption period has expired, the association heard that there was news of continued collection, and has submitted a report to the central government and the competent authorities on the state of decline of the Shandong coal mining industry, and based on the order of the Executive Yuan to the provincial and municipal governments that no additional coal tax should be levied except for statutory taxes, requesting that the temporary fee be exempted as soon as possible to relieve merchants.

Surrenders to the Patrol Station After the Incident

Mu Shouren, a scoundrel from Shandong, 38 years old, and Wang Yuyao, a doorman patrol from Tianjin at 780 Zhonghui Bank, 97 Avenue Edward in the French Concession, were fellow disciples. Mu often went to Wang to borrow money. Wang initially used polite words to provide a small amount of assistance, but Mu regarded Wang as owing it to him. The head of the patrol saw that he had no obvious criminal behavior and immediately reprimanded him and dismissed him. Unexpectedly, at about 10:00 a.m. today, Mu went again and forcibly demanded money. Wang could no longer tolerate it and pulled out his pistol to threaten him. Business Plummets

丨This Is an Inevitable Phenomenon丨

Recently, the dance halls run by Japanese in this port have been deserted and silent after the exchange rate plummeted, except for the dance halls in coffee shops that do not charge fees. Therefore, in order to alleviate the situation, the operators plan to reduce ticket prices or abolish the music team and replace it with an electric phonograph. All dance tickets sold in the past were only three for one yuan, but now they can be bought for five at a lower price. On the one hand, the monthly salary system will now be changed to a weekly proportional income system, and the expansion of various restaurants and dance halls will be restricted.

Talks

Why Doesn't Matsuoka Commit Suicide? 143

— Me

In the year of Guiyou, the Xiongnu invaded the south, occupied the most important pass in the world and massacred Chaoyang, peeped into Beijing and Tianjin, and wanted to occupy the Central Plains. It seemed that the world could not be peaceful without destroying China. The whole country was in panic, and no one dared to resist the enemy. At this time, the European and American powers, with their foresight, did not want the great fat to be swallowed alone by the beast. Therefore, they issued their "non-heavenly pity" grand wish, chanting words in their mouths, and gathering the philosophy of the sages into chapters. After passing through the Nineteen Committees, they passed through the General Assembly of the League of Nations. From then on, the patriotic people of our country, as well as the gentlemen, all put their hands on their foreheads and congratulated each other, saying, "Justice is fortunately extended, and public opinion is more manifested. If it were not for our people's efforts to seek spiritual resistance, could we have obtained such a great victory?" It can be known that the upper and lower classes congratulated each other. However, Matsuoka, the chief representative on the other hand, could not be so happy. The reason is that the international elders are not willing to let Japan monopolize the Northeast. They want the Japanese army to withdraw to the Manchurian Railway area and establish an international police force to maintain the security of China's territory. Therefore, the Japanese Empire cannot avoid losing face. Therefore, Matsuoka Yosuke cannot avoid leaving Geneva with "sorrow and disappointment."

But I still remember that at the beginning of Matsuoka's appointment as chief representative, he had the determination to sacrifice himself for the country. In order to confirm that my memory is still sound, I found the following record in the old newspaper piles.

The Far East News Agency, Osaka, 18th: Recently, the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun published Matsuoka Yosuke's hard work in Geneva, saying that when Matsuoka left the country for Geneva, his old mother personally presented him with a Japanese sword and told him to fight for the country, saying that if diplomacy failed in the League of Nations, he could commit suicide with the sword to show the spirit of the Yamato nation. Since the League of Nations General Assembly, Japanese diplomacy has gradually fallen into a stalemate. Matsuoka often showed signs of regret when he returned to his residence. He often opened the box and looked at the sword given by his mother and sighed. Therefore, a group of entourages are worried that Matsuoka will commit suicide.

According to the above record, Matsuoka should have obeyed his mother's order to "commit suicide to show the spirit of the Yamato nation" in order to be worthy of being a filial son and martyr. But he did not commit suicide, and a group of entourages were worried in vain, but only "left with sorrow and disappointment." And only said in self-explanation, "If I did not have the perseverance of an Oriental, I would definitely cry for it." In this way, the spirit of the Yamato nation cannot avoid being weakened. Alas, if I were a Japanese, "I would definitely cry for it."

Then, why doesn't Matsuoka commit suicide? Of course, he has his reasons. The first is that the representative of Siam gave up the right to vote on the resolution. This point cannot avoid being "what he is pleased with." At least, his diplomacy has not completely failed, so he can still avoid committing suicide. Secondly, the great powers' resolution to jointly manage the Northeast did not dare to clearly exclude Japan. Under the name of "Chinese sovereignty," Japanese imperialism can still open its bloody mouth and devour a large number of the Chinese working masses, but it cannot be full alone. Therefore, Matsuoka's diplomacy is still successful and does not disgrace the emperor's order, so of course, he can avoid committing suicide even more.

Looking at it this way, the reasons for Matsuoka's not committing suicide are still sufficient, and the Chinese nation will never transcend its colonial status because of his suicide. Therefore, we the public can only commit suicide, arm ourselves, and seek our own liberation in the thorough anti-imperialist national revolutionary war.

Arts and Literature

Responding to "Giving Charcoal in the Snow" 144

— Sun Choucheng

A friend gave me a poem about sending coal to the refugees in Hualin Mountain after the snow, and asked me to respond to it. (The original poem has been published in this journal on the 1st of this month.) I respond to it according to the rhyme.

Alas, my fellow villagers, the soldiers have robbed them during the drought. Not yet three hundred years, they have suffered from famine nine times. (From the year of Shunzhi Wuzi to the present three hundred years, the river bandits have rebelled a total of nine times.) Some were burned overnight, and some were scattered in all directions. Those who fled sold their children for food, and those who were besieged dissected their bones for food. Those who went far away flowed to Tao and Min, and who gave them shelter on their poor journey? Those who came to the provincial capital, who watered their hungry intestines? Fortunately, there are wise men in the world who control happiness and suffering. They give porridge and clothes to avoid the invasion of cold. However, the heaven and man are blocked, and the heavy snow has submerged their shins. When will the bandits be suppressed? They endure the cold through the night. Only worry about the river water freezing hard, and the success or failure is difficult to predict. My friend Deng Zhonghua sighed at this. He wants to help the people after the robbery, and send charcoal in the snow to all of them. How can we get a generous family, and everyone will pity and embrace the rare?

Saving the Nation with Beauty 145

— Little Fellow

In such a year of "saving the nation," filled with fanfare and lively excitement, the ways to save the nation are truly too numerous to recount in one breath. Look, from "non-resistance to save the nation" to "aviation to save the nation," "motor to save the nation," "mantras to save the nation," "antiques to save the nation," "sports to save the nation," "machine gun to save the nation," "golf to save the nation," "morphine to save the nation," "dancing to save the nation," "entertainment to save the nation," "mahjong to save the nation," "prostitutes to save the nation," "La Dame aux Camélias to save the nation"... And then, there's the "saving the nation with beauty" by Ms. Chen Biyun of Hong Kong, which was shockingly published with a decorative border in the newspaper not long ago. Whew, I recited it too quickly and rapidly; I almost choked, this little fellow did!

When I discovered this "1933" style new term, this new path of "saving the nation with beauty," amidst my ecstatic joy and leaping three hundred, jumping five thousand times, tears welled up and soaked my coarse cloth gown. My friends were astonished and asked, "Where did this come from?" I told them, "My dear people, you are so pitiful, how can you be so foolish? Let me tell you, our motherland has yet another way to be saved! My tears, these tears, are tears of joy!" And so, after two days, or perhaps more than two days, my friends happily brought me Mr. Geng's two pieces of earnest and heartfelt, bodhisattva-like praise and advocacy for this "1933" new method of "saving the nation," to read to me. I closed my eyes, held my breath, and after listening quietly, I clapped my hands and stomped my feet, shouting in a melodious voice, "Wonderful, wonderful!" Indeed, if it weren't for my inherent thick skin, I would have gladly sold my pants belt to buy a pound or two of lead powder to "jade" up this "beauty," because this is a grand undertaking related to "saving" our riddled mother"land." However, what can be done? Is "thick skin saving the nation" even possible in this era? And so, I became somewhat indignant.

Ultimately, this attitude is incorrect. Others are burying their heads in makeup to "save the nation," while I am not looking for a way, but merely being "indignant," "indignant" about what? Forget it, let's cool down this brain, "eliminate prejudices," "overcome national difficulties together," and research the convenient and remarkably effective methods for implementing this new type of "saving the nation." And so, after my repeated trials and four attempts and seven failures, I finally discovered the following three self-evident principles with great pleasure. Friends, you are comrades enthusiastic about saving the nation, come, let's play with them together with one heart and one mind.

(1) Undoubtedly, "saving the nation with beauty" can greatly raise a sum of money to buy large quantities of military firearms to give to the "Volunteer Army" to fight the Japanese. However, I propose that we should not rush to use this "raised" sum of money to buy

Page 22

military firearms for the "Volunteer Army" to fight the Japanese. We can use this money as capital to establish a large-scale "Beauty to Save the Nation Training Institute," divided into accelerated and regular courses. The reason is that this can broadly attract talent, provide training, and in the future, graduates can become a large group of "Beauty to Save the Nation," and then each member can use their "beauty" to raise money, so wouldn't there be more money and wouldn't there be an inexhaustible supply of military firearms? (2) Young men should give money to women who "save the nation with beauty," and when faced with reproaches from parents or condemnations from moralists, they should use this strong and powerful reason of "saving the nation," fully explain it, enlighten them with righteousness, and scold them three times as pigs who do not know the hatred of national subjugation.

(3) As for the third method, please forgive me for keeping it a secret from you, esteemed readers. If you want to know what the third method actually is, please wait until the entire "Volunteer Army" gathers in Qiqihar, then passes through Tomsk, and finally fights its way to our Shanghai, before I reveal it.
