Clerk Communication

House Arrest 146

— Sun Yihe

Editor:

Thank you, please help me solve a difficult problem! I am an employee of a somewhat foreign-style national goods store. Ten years ago, I left school and said goodbye to my parents to become an apprentice at this store. The colleagues in the store are all from this store's apprentices. Our master, that is, our boss, treats us very well on the surface; our monthly salary is only about ten yuan; but if you are short of expenses, he will agree to lend you ten or twenty yuan each month; sometimes when there are weddings or funerals in our family, he will never refuse to lend us two or three hundred yuan. How grateful we were at that time! Therefore, in these ten years, I have accumulated a debt of more than eight hundred yuan, and in the future, I estimate that I will still accumulate at least one hundred yuan each year! He accumulates the debts year after year in the account book; we also turn a blind eye.

This year, I found a position with a higher salary, so I pleaded with the boss, asking him to allow me to resign; unexpectedly, his reply sounded very benevolent and righteous, but in essence, it was very harmful. He said, "People look up to high mountains and water looks down to low places. Now that you have a better job, it is certainly inconvenient to keep you here; but my business has a small capital, and a debt of more than eight hundred yuan must be repaid by you in advance. Otherwise, please stay here and suffer for a while, because it is absolutely impossible to lend money to an unrelated person!" At this point, I realized that he was using the method of "house arrest"!

Editor, there is no future here for a lifetime! But I don't have the power to repay the debt first and then resign. As for deliberately doing a few things that violate store rules to make him fire me; I am not willing to try this shameless behavior. Then, do I have other ways to break through this prison of "house arrest"? (Omitted below)

Sun Yihe bows

Editor's note: We received Mr. Sun's letter and discussed it with many people who are experienced in the business world; we know that many shopkeepers are adopting this method of "house arrest." At the same time, we believe that although the methods adopted by these shopkeepers are erroneous, their motives cannot be erased. They at least have two good intentions: "love of talent" and "consideration." Therefore, we are specifically discussing it publicly here, hoping that shopkeepers with these good intentions will find other ways.

It is understandable that shopkeepers want their useful partners to work for them for a long time and not help other colleagues to become their strong enemies. However, the method of winning people over must be generous. If you can be considerate of their treatment, then people are not made of wood or stone, and they will of course do their best. If Mr. Sun's shopkeeper can openly and rightly use the money owed to each as salary, it can be calculated that Mr. Sun's monthly salary, except for the first three years of apprenticeship, can also be about thirty yuan per month. I think Mr. Sun can of course live in peace and will not have the idea of ​​seeing different and moving. Now, although he actually has an income of thirty yuan a month, because he nominally bears a large amount of debt, of course he feels uneasy and is eager to seek another job. Fortunately, Mr. Sun is a decent person, so he is not willing to deliberately violate store rules, otherwise you will regret it too late. We advise Mr. Sun to understand the shopkeeper's good intentions and negotiate with the boss once; add some to the previous salary, settle on the amount owed; and at the same time, please increase the salary in the future and set a method of repayment in installments. Then, such a considerate old master, the new master may not be able to surpass, you may wish to cancel the idea of ​​seeking another job. If he cannot do so, you can go to him. Fortunately, this kind of debt is the money he voluntarily lent, unlike the private collection of customer accounts and other money, which violates criminal law. The law is nothing more than human sentiment, even if you sue in court, it will at most be discounted and repaid in installments.

Clerk Communication Column Regulations 147

(1) The purpose of the communication is to gather wisdom, explain difficult problems, hone each other, and enhance the happiness of life. (2) The target of the communication is limited to clerks and apprentices in terms of people, and limited to this city in terms of location. (3) The content of the communication includes everything about personal daily life, such as:

(1) Occupation (2) Moral and academic cultivation (3) Entertainment and sports (4) Marriage, as well as other issues related to the country and society, are all welcome. If the content of the question is too profound and beyond the ability of this column, it can also be introduced to this newspaper's "Reader Questions, Answered on Behalf."

(4) Method of Submission

(1) The name, age, native place, occupation, and detailed contact information must be clearly stated at the end of the letter; this must still be stated in subsequent letters.

Novel

Coal Mountain (Continued) 148

— By Ep Falkowski, Abridged and Translated by Zhixiang

(V)

On Monday morning, the crushing sound, as if vehicles heavily loaded with bricks collided with each other, filled the entire city. Monday, the sound of explosions in the mine echoed in the valley. Monday, awakened the miners who were sleeping soundly in bed: urging them to put on their rubber shoes and move towards the mine.

Drinking, smoking, singing, Saturday night and Sunday, struggle and hope, earning money and spending money, constantly struggling in impoverished huts, paying rent, giving birth to children, workers being crushed or injured in the mine, old miners planning how to work in the mine to make a living 丨 Everything, everything, ended and started on Monday morning. The terrible whistle of the mine urged countless miners to send their priceless lives into the mine. The miners dug coal, digging with all their strength; the managers only hoped to obtain profits, more profits.

On that dismal Monday, the workers were not allowed to talk, they were as if sealed off and unable to speak. The newspapers were full of news of the recession 丨 the market was shrinking, but the managers and foremen were still frantically demanding coal. The ominous headline read: "No longer needed", which had already made the entire coal industry depressed; and this terrible phenomenon continued to spread. The period of layoffs had arrived: the workers were afraid of job insecurity, not knowing which day would be their last day of work. But, the urgent work of mining coal was still progressing; the hateful foreman frantically urged the workers to dig coal in sweat, and even more tons of coal.

Ten poor workers, boarding the elevator, they felt the cold wind coming from the darkness below. Trembling flames stretched out from the kerosene lamp. They listened quietly to the sound of running water, the spire of the house where the crusher was placed, showing a line of azure sky, heavy frost covered the track, uneven iron plates on the explosives room, oil room and ticket office 丨 the place where the workers checked their numbers when they went to work in the mine. The frost along the sloping roof of the crusher reflected the light. Tense silence filled everything.

Peter stood on the elevator covered with mud. In the trembling light, he looked at the thin and haggard faces of his companions. The bell rang, the elevator descended rapidly: a sharp sound rolled into the eardrum, and the brain also felt tense. The sound of iron chains, the sound of the elevator and the wooden strips next to it rubbing against each other, sent into the eardrum in bursts, descending, down. Until that dark and dangerous place; but, here are buried countless treasures∶∶∶∶∶∶.

Vehicles heavily loaded with coal were waiting below. The miners rushed through the curtain made by the rapids, stepping into the smelly tunnel. A cold wind came from the top of the tunnel. Peter followed a line of clear light and proceeded along the difficult tunnel. An old mule driving a cart stood in front, and a companion with a face covered with mud stood beside him, chewing bread. Peter ran to the small path that could only be walked by one person; when walking from there to another slope, he had to hold on to the wooden stakes tightly. The dim stones, as if angered by the light revealing their secrets, often stabbed the workers' hands; the rough wooden stakes also often hooked the workers'

clothes. Indescribable danger was tensely approaching in the darkness step by step. Darkness had its own life 丨 it had its own nightmares, sorrows, laughter, plans; terrible malice and bitter feelings; it would flatter people, ridicule people, caress people; poison people, destroy people. It was forever silent, except when sporadic stones rolled into

the tunnel, or when explosives exploded,
